# System T

We start off by defining the language that we will
use to showcase normalization by evaluation, System T,
as is done in Section 2.1.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="154" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="161" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html" class="Module">Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality</a> <a id="199" class="Symbol">as</a> <a id="202" class="Module">Eq</a>

<a id="327" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="332" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="339" href="Data.Product.html" class="Module">Data.Product</a> <a id="352" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="358" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="359" href="Data.Product.html#1167" class="Function Operator">_×_</a><a id="362" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="364" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">proj₁</a><a id="369" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="371" href="Data.Product.html#1369" class="Function">∃</a><a id="372" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="374" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">∃-syntax</a><a id="382" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">renaming</a> <a id="393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="394" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="398" class="Symbol">to</a> <a id="401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨_,_⟩</a><a id="406" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="408" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="413" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="420" href="Relation.Nullary.html" class="Module">Relation.Nullary</a> <a id="437" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="443" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="444" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1511" class="Record">Dec</a><a id="447" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="449" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1648" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a><a id="452" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="454" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1685" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a><a id="456" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="458" href="Relation.Nullary.html#656" class="Function Operator">¬_</a><a id="460" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="488" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="493" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html" class="Module">Eq</a> <a id="496" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="503" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#208" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="507" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="509" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#151" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a><a id="512" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="514" class="Keyword">renaming</a> <a id="523" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="524" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1684" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="528" class="Symbol">to</a> <a id="531" class="Function">≡-sym</a><a id="536" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="538" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1729" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="544" class="Symbol">to</a> <a id="547" class="Function">≡-trans</a><a id="554" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="557" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="564" href="NbE.html" class="Module">NbE</a> <a id="568" class="Keyword">where</a>
</pre>
It has natural numbers, higher-order functions, and
primitive recursion. We will define it with intrinsic
typing, and use a de Brujin index representation
for variables.

We start off with the types of tha language: naturals
and functions.

</pre>
We continue with typing contexts, defined inductively
with the empty context, and extensions to contexts. As
we are using a de Brujin index representation, there
are no names when extending contexts (and really they
are just lists of types).
<pre class="Agda"><a id="1719" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Ctx"></a><a id="1724" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="1728" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1730" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="1734" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="2265" class="Symbol">...</a>                      <a id="2290" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="2292" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1648" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="2296" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#208" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>  <a id="2302" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="2304" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1648" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="2308" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#208" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="2313" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2315" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1648" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="2319" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#208" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>
We also define a relation detailing when one context is the
extension of another, this is introduced formally in a later
section but will be useful throughout. A context is an extension
of itself, and given that one context Γ′ extends another context
Γ, the first can be extended further and the relation will still hold.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="2659" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_≤_"></a><a id="2664" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">_≤_</a> <a id="2668" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2670" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="2674" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2676" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="2680" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2682" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="2686" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="_≤_.≤-id"></a><a id="2694" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a> <a id="2699" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2701" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2703" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2704" href="NbE.html#2704" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2706" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2708" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="2711" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2713" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2715" href="NbE.html#2704" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2717" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="2719" href="NbE.html#2704" class="Bound">Γ</a>

  <a id="_≤_.≤-ext"></a><a id="2724" href="NbE.html#2724" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-ext</a> <a id="2730" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2732" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2734" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2735" href="NbE.html#2735" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="2737" href="NbE.html#2737" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="2740" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2742" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="2745" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2747" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2748" href="NbE.html#2748" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2752" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="2756" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="2766" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2768" href="NbE.html#2737" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="2771" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="2773" href="NbE.html#2735" class="Bound">Γ</a>

        <a id="2804" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2806" href="NbE.html#2737" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="2809" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2811" href="NbE.html#2748" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2813" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="2815" href="NbE.html#2735" class="Bound">Γ</a>

</pre>
We also introduce a lookup judgement for
contexts, which corresponds to a de Brujin
index.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="3450" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_∋_"></a><a id="3455" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">_∋_</a> <a id="3459" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3461" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="3465" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3467" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="3472" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3474" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="3478" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="_∋_.`Z"></a><a id="3486" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="3489" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3491" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3493" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3494" href="NbE.html#3494" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3496" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3498" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="3501" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3503" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3504" href="NbE.html#3504" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="3506" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3508" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="3512" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="3522" class="Comment">---------</a>
      <a id="3538" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3540" href="NbE.html#3494" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3542" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3544" href="NbE.html#3504" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="3546" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="3548" href="NbE.html#3504" class="Bound">T</a>

  <a id="_∋_.`S_"></a><a id="3553" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S_</a> <a id="3557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3559" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3561" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3562" href="NbE.html#3562" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3564" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3566" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="3569" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3571" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3572" href="NbE.html#3572" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="3574" href="NbE.html#3574" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="3576" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3578" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="3582" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="3590" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3592" href="NbE.html#3562" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3594" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="3596" href="NbE.html#3574" class="Bound">T</a>
        <a id="3606" class="Comment">---------</a>
      <a id="3622" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3624" href="NbE.html#3562" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3626" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3628" href="NbE.html#3572" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="3630" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="3632" href="NbE.html#3574" class="Bound">T</a>

<a id="3635" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="3641" class="Number">4</a> <a id="3643" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">_∋_</a>
</pre>
Terms in our language are defined with an intrinsically
typed represenation, such that a term t of type Γ ⊢ T is
the term `Γ ⊢ t : T` itself. The language has the constants `zero`,
`suc` (as a curried constant),`rec` (a curried constant
as well), variables, abstractions, and application.

For clarity we will not use an intrinsically typed de Brujin
representation when talking about terms (e.g. the variable ` `Z
will be talked about as `Γ , x:T ⊢ x : T`)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="4118" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_⊢_"></a><a id="4123" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">_⊢_</a> <a id="4127" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4128" href="NbE.html#4128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4130" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4132" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="4135" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4137" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4139" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="4144" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4146" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="4150" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="_⊢_.zero"></a><a id="4158" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="4163" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4165" href="NbE.html#4128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4167" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4169" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a>

  <a id="_⊢_.`_"></a><a id="4308" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`_</a> <a id="4311" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4313" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="4315" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4316" href="NbE.html#4316" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="4318" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4320" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="4324" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="4331" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4333" href="NbE.html#4128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4335" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="4337" href="NbE.html#4316" class="Bound">S</a>

       <a id="4412" class="Comment">---------</a>
     <a id="4427" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4429" href="NbE.html#4128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4431" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4433" href="NbE.html#4376" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="4435" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="4437" href="NbE.html#4378" class="Bound">T</a>

  <a id="_⊢_._·_"></a><a id="4442" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="4446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4448" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="4450" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4451" href="NbE.html#4451" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="4453" href="NbE.html#4453" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="4455" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4457" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="4461" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="4469" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4471" href="NbE.html#4128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4473" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4475" href="NbE.html#4451" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="4477" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="4479" href="NbE.html#4453" class="Bound">T</a>
      <a id="4487" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4489" href="NbE.html#4128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4491" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4493" href="NbE.html#4451" class="Bound">S</a>
        <a id="4503" class="Comment">---------</a>
      <a id="4519" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4521" href="NbE.html#4128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4523" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4525" href="NbE.html#4453" class="Bound">T</a>

<a id="4528" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="4534" class="Number">4</a> <a id="4536" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">_⊢_</a>
<a id="4540" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="4546" class="Number">5</a> <a id="4548" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a>
<a id="4551" class="Keyword">infixl</a> <a id="4558" class="Number">7</a> <a id="4560" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a>
<a id="4564" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="4570" class="Number">9</a> <a id="4572" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`_</a>
</pre>
We can define some sample programs in the language
using these constructors:
<pre class="Agda"><a id="4665" class="Comment">-- λx. x</a>
<a id="ex0"></a><a id="4674" href="NbE.html#4674" class="Function">ex0</a> <a id="4678" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4680" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="4682" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4683" href="NbE.html#4683" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4685" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4687" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="4690" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4692" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4693" href="NbE.html#4693" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="4695" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4697" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="4701" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4703" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4705" href="NbE.html#4683" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4707" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4709" href="NbE.html#4693" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="4711" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="4713" href="NbE.html#4693" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="4715" href="NbE.html#4674" class="Function">ex0</a> <a id="4719" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4721" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="4723" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="4725" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4726" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a><a id="4728" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="4731" class="Comment">-- (λx. x) zero</a>
<a id="ex1"></a><a id="4747" href="NbE.html#4747" class="Function">ex1</a> <a id="4751" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4753" href="NbE.html#4674" class="Function">ex0</a> <a id="4757" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="4759" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="4764" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4765" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a><a id="4766" class="Symbol">}</a>

<a id="4769" class="Comment">-- suc ((λx. x) zero)</a>
<a id="ex2"></a><a id="4791" href="NbE.html#4791" class="Function">ex2</a> <a id="4795" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4797" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="4801" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="4803" href="NbE.html#4747" class="Function">ex1</a>

<a id="4808" class="Comment">-- x:nat, y:nat ⊢ suc ((λz. suc y) x)</a>
<a id="ex3"></a><a id="4846" href="NbE.html#4846" class="Function">ex3</a> <a id="4850" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4852" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="4854" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4856" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="4860" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4862" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="4866" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4868" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a>
<a id="4872" href="NbE.html#4846" class="Function">ex3</a> <a id="4876" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4878" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="4882" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="4884" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="4886" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="4888" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="4892" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="4894" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="4896" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4897" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="4900" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a><a id="4902" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4905" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="4907" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="4909" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4910" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="4913" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a><a id="4915" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
Now that we have defined our language, we are almost ready
to start describing an algorithm for normalization by
evaluation. However, to prove the soundness of this algorithm,
we will need to define two more basic language constructs:
substitutions and equality.

We expect the following soundness properties for a
normalization algorithm nf(t) that produces a normal form
for a typed term `Γ ⊢ t : T`:

  - `Γ ⊢ nf(t) : T` (well-typedness of normal form)
  - `⟦ nf(t) ⟧ = ⟦ t ⟧` (preservation of meaning)
  - `nf(nf(t)) = nf(t)` (idempotency)

For preservation of meaning, our interpretations of
functional terms are functions, whose equality is
undecidable. However, in STLC, we have that two terms
are βη-equivalent iff their interpretationss are equal.
So, we wish to define an extension of βη-equivalence
for System T s.t. it implies equal interpretations
(thus making the proposition `⟦ nf(t) ⟧ = ⟦ t ⟧` decidable).

To define our extension of βη-equivalence, we begin by
defining substitution (which we will use to define β-reductions
and η-expansions).

Substitution for System T is defined using the rules for
parallel substitution and the rule for the application
of a substitution as they are introduced in section 2.6.

A parallel substitution `Γ ⊢ σ : Δ` provides a well-typed term in Γ
to substitute for each variable in the context Δ.

We use ⊩ instead of ⊢ since that is already reserved
for typing judgements (and keep using ∥ for the "parallel"
in "parallel substitutions" for operationsions related
to this type).
<pre class="Agda"><a id="6464" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Sub"></a><a id="6469" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="6473" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6475" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="6479" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6481" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="6485" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6487" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="6491" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Sub.∅"></a><a id="6499" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="6501" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6503" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6505" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6506" href="NbE.html#6506" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="6507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6509" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6511" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="6515" href="NbE.html#6506" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6517" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>

  <a id="Sub._,_"></a><a id="6522" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="6526" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6528" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6530" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6531" href="NbE.html#6531" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6533" href="NbE.html#6533" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="6535" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6537" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="6540" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6542" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6543" href="NbE.html#6543" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="6545" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6547" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="6551" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="6561" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6563" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="6567" href="NbE.html#6531" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6569" href="NbE.html#6533" class="Bound">Δ</a>
        <a id="6579" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6581" href="NbE.html#6531" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6583" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="6585" href="NbE.html#6543" class="Bound">S</a>
          <a id="6597" class="Comment">---------</a>
        <a id="6615" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6617" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="6621" href="NbE.html#6531" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6623" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6624" href="NbE.html#6533" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="6626" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="6628" href="NbE.html#6543" class="Bound">S</a><a id="6629" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Before defining the application of a substitution
`Γ ⊢ t [ σ ] : `T, we introduce renaming.

Renaming is a specialized substitution where
we can only substitute variables with other
variables (i.e. a renaming `Γ ⊢ σᵣ : Δ` provides
a variable in Γ to replace for every variable in Δ).

It is necessary to first to define renaming substitutions
so that termination is guaranteed for our operations.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="7041" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Ren"></a><a id="7046" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="7050" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7052" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="7056" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7058" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="7062" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7064" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="7068" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Ren.∅"></a><a id="7076" href="NbE.html#7076" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="7078" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7080" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7082" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7083" href="NbE.html#7083" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7085" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7087" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="7090" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7092" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7094" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="7098" href="NbE.html#7083" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7100" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>

  <a id="Ren._,_"></a><a id="7105" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="7109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7111" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7113" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7114" href="NbE.html#7114" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7116" href="NbE.html#7116" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="7118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7120" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="7123" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7125" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7126" href="NbE.html#7126" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="7128" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7130" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="7134" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="7142" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7144" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="7148" href="NbE.html#7114" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7150" href="NbE.html#7116" class="Bound">Δ</a>
      <a id="7158" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7160" href="NbE.html#7114" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7162" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="7164" href="NbE.html#7126" class="Bound">S</a>
        <a id="7174" class="Comment">-------------</a>
      <a id="7194" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7196" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="7200" href="NbE.html#7114" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7202" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7203" href="NbE.html#7116" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="7205" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7207" href="NbE.html#7126" class="Bound">S</a><a id="7208" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
We can use a renaming substitution to convert
lookup judgements (i.e. rename variables). In fact, this
is the operation that we need to define separately to
guarantee termination of the application of a substitution.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="rename"></a><a id="7440" href="NbE.html#7440" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="7447" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7449" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7451" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7452" href="NbE.html#7452" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7454" href="NbE.html#7454" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="7456" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7458" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="7461" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7463" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7464" href="NbE.html#7464" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="7466" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7468" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="7472" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="7481" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7483" href="NbE.html#7454" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="7485" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="7487" href="NbE.html#7464" class="Bound">T</a>
       <a id="7496" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7498" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="7502" href="NbE.html#7452" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7504" href="NbE.html#7454" class="Bound">Δ</a>
         <a id="7515" class="Comment">-------</a>
       <a id="7530" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7532" href="NbE.html#7452" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7534" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="7536" href="NbE.html#7464" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="7538" href="NbE.html#7440" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="7545" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a>     <a id="7552" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7553" href="NbE.html#7553" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="7555" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7557" href="NbE.html#7557" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7558" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7560" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7562" href="NbE.html#7557" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="7564" href="NbE.html#7440" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="7571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7572" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="7575" href="NbE.html#7575" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7576" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7579" href="NbE.html#7579" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="7581" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7583" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="7586" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7588" href="NbE.html#7440" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="7595" href="NbE.html#7575" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7597" href="NbE.html#7579" class="Bound">ρ</a>
</pre>
We define parallel substitutions and renaming substitutions
with the previous rules so that we can define a shifting operation
over them. Shifting a renaming substitution shifts all indices
in the renaming by one -- in other words, given a renaming between Γ
and Δ, we can create a renaming between Γ , T and Δ.

We will use this to extend a renaming under a binder.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_↑ᵣ"></a><a id="7979" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">_↑ᵣ</a> <a id="7983" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7985" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7987" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7988" href="NbE.html#7988" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7990" href="NbE.html#7990" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="7992" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7994" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="7997" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7999" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8000" href="NbE.html#8000" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="8002" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8004" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="8008" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="8014" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8016" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="8020" href="NbE.html#7988" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8022" href="NbE.html#7990" class="Bound">Δ</a>
      <a id="8030" class="Comment">-------------</a>
    <a id="8048" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8050" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="8054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8055" href="NbE.html#7988" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8057" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8059" href="NbE.html#8000" class="Bound">T</a><a id="8060" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8062" href="NbE.html#7990" class="Bound">Δ</a>
<a id="8064" href="NbE.html#7076" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="8066" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">↑ᵣ</a>       <a id="8075" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8077" href="NbE.html#7076" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>
<a id="8079" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8080" href="NbE.html#8080" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8083" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8085" href="NbE.html#8085" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8086" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8088" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">↑ᵣ</a> <a id="8091" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8093" href="NbE.html#8080" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8096" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">↑ᵣ</a> <a id="8099" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8101" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="8104" href="NbE.html#8085" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="8107" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="8113" class="Number">6</a> <a id="8115" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">_↑ᵣ</a>
</pre>
With this operation in place, we can define the application of a renaming
substitution to rebase a term from a context Δ to a context Γ, this is done
by using the renaming substitution to replace all variables used in the term by
their corresponding variables in Γ
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_[_]ᵣ"></a><a id="8397" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">_[_]ᵣ</a> <a id="8403" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8405" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="8407" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8408" href="NbE.html#8408" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8410" href="NbE.html#8410" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="8412" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8414" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="8417" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8419" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8420" href="NbE.html#8420" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="8422" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8424" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="8428" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="8438" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8440" href="NbE.html#8410" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="8442" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="8444" href="NbE.html#8420" class="Bound">T</a>
        <a id="8454" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8456" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="8460" href="NbE.html#8408" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8462" href="NbE.html#8410" class="Bound">Δ</a>
          <a id="8474" class="Comment">-------</a>
        <a id="8490" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8492" href="NbE.html#8408" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8494" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="8496" href="NbE.html#8420" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="8498" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="8503" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8505" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8507" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a> <a id="8510" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8512" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>

<a id="8534" href="NbE.html#4199" class="InductiveConstructor">rec</a> <a id="8538" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8540" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8542" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a> <a id="8545" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8547" href="NbE.html#4199" class="InductiveConstructor">rec</a>
<a id="8551" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="8553" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="8556" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8558" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8560" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8562" href="NbE.html#8562" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8564" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a> <a id="8567" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8569" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="8571" href="NbE.html#8562" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="8573" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="8575" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="8578" href="NbE.html#8578" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8580" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8582" href="NbE.html#8582" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8585" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8587" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8589" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a> <a id="8592" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8594" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="8596" href="NbE.html#8578" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8598" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8600" href="NbE.html#8582" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8603" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a>
<a id="8606" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8607" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="8609" href="NbE.html#8609" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8610" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8612" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8614" href="NbE.html#8614" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8617" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a> <a id="8620" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8622" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="8624" href="NbE.html#8609" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8626" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8628" href="NbE.html#8614" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8631" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">↑ᵣ</a> <a id="8634" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8636" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="8639" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a>
<a id="8642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8643" href="NbE.html#8643" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="8645" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="8647" href="NbE.html#8647" class="Bound">s</a><a id="8648" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8650" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8652" href="NbE.html#8652" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8655" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a> <a id="8658" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8660" href="NbE.html#8643" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="8662" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8664" href="NbE.html#8652" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8667" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a> <a id="8670" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="8672" href="NbE.html#8647" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="8674" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="8676" href="NbE.html#8652" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="8679" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a>

<a id="8683" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="8689" class="Number">8</a> <a id="8691" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">_[_]ᵣ</a>
</pre>
We also define a few "primitive" renamings that will be convenient for general
substitutions:

The identity and incrementing renaming, defined mutually. The identity
renaming leaves all variables unchanged, while the incrementing renaming
increments all variables (which are really just indices) by 1

<pre class="Agda"><a id="9012" class="Keyword">mutual</a>
  <a id="ren-id"></a><a id="9021" href="NbE.html#9021" class="Function">ren-id</a> <a id="9028" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9030" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9032" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9033" href="NbE.html#9033" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9035" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9037" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="9040" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9042" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9044" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="9048" href="NbE.html#9033" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9050" href="NbE.html#9033" class="Bound">Γ</a>
  <a id="9054" href="NbE.html#9021" class="Function">ren-id</a> <a id="9061" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9062" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a><a id="9063" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9065" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9067" href="NbE.html#7076" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>
  <a id="9071" href="NbE.html#9021" class="Function">ren-id</a> <a id="9078" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9079" href="NbE.html#9079" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9081" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9083" href="NbE.html#9083" class="Bound">T</a><a id="9084" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9086" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9088" href="NbE.html#9105" class="Function">ren-incr</a> <a id="9097" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9099" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a>

  <a id="ren-incr"></a><a id="9105" href="NbE.html#9105" class="Function">ren-incr</a> <a id="9114" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9116" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9118" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9119" href="NbE.html#9119" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9123" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="9126" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9128" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9129" href="NbE.html#9129" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="9131" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9133" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="9137" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9139" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9141" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="9145" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9146" href="NbE.html#9119" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9148" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9150" href="NbE.html#9129" class="Bound">T</a><a id="9151" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9153" href="NbE.html#9119" class="Bound">Γ</a>
  <a id="9157" href="NbE.html#9105" class="Function">ren-incr</a> <a id="9166" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9168" href="NbE.html#9021" class="Function">ren-id</a> <a id="9175" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">↑ᵣ</a>
</pre>
A renaming between a context Γ′ and Γ,
where Γ′ is an extension of Γ. This renaming
is really a series of shifts based on
how many extensions to Γ the context Γ′
contains.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ren-≤"></a><a id="9364" href="NbE.html#9364" class="Function">ren-≤</a> <a id="9370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9372" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9374" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9375" href="NbE.html#9375" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="9378" href="NbE.html#9378" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9382" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="9385" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9387" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9389" href="NbE.html#9375" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="9392" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="9394" href="NbE.html#9378" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9396" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9398" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="9402" href="NbE.html#9375" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="9405" href="NbE.html#9378" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="9407" href="NbE.html#9364" class="Function">ren-≤</a> <a id="9413" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a> <a id="9418" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9420" href="NbE.html#9021" class="Function">ren-id</a>
<a id="9427" href="NbE.html#9364" class="Function">ren-≤</a> <a id="9433" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9434" href="NbE.html#2724" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-ext</a> <a id="9440" href="NbE.html#9440" class="Bound">pf</a><a id="9442" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9444" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9447" href="NbE.html#9364" class="Function">ren-≤</a> <a id="9453" href="NbE.html#9440" class="Bound">pf</a><a id="9455" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9457" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">↑ᵣ</a>
</pre>
Since a renaming is really just a specialized substitution,
we can transform any renaming substitution into a parallel
substitution
<pre class="Agda"><a id="subst-ren"></a><a id="9605" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="9615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9617" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9619" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9620" href="NbE.html#9620" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9622" href="NbE.html#9622" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="9624" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9626" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="9629" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9633" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="9637" href="NbE.html#9620" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9639" href="NbE.html#9622" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="9641" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9643" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="9647" href="NbE.html#9620" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9649" href="NbE.html#9622" class="Bound">Δ</a>
<a id="9651" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="9661" href="NbE.html#7076" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="9663" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9665" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>
<a id="9667" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="9677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9678" href="NbE.html#9678" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="9681" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9683" href="NbE.html#9683" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9684" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9686" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9688" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="9698" href="NbE.html#9678" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="9701" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9703" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="9705" href="NbE.html#9683" class="Bound">x</a>
</pre>
We can now use our renaming substitutions to build out
parallel substitutions and their operations, such that
their operations are guaranteed to terminate.

Similarly as for renaming substitutions, we define a shifting
operation for parallel substitutions, to be used for extending
a substitution under a binder.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_↑"></a><a id="10033" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">_↑</a> <a id="10036" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10038" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10040" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10041" href="NbE.html#10041" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10043" href="NbE.html#10043" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="10045" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10047" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="10050" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10052" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10053" href="NbE.html#10053" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="10055" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10057" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="10061" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="10069" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10071" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="10075" href="NbE.html#10041" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10077" href="NbE.html#10043" class="Bound">Δ</a>
        <a id="10087" class="Comment">-------------</a>
      <a id="10107" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10109" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="10113" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10114" href="NbE.html#10041" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10116" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10118" href="NbE.html#10053" class="Bound">T</a><a id="10119" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10121" href="NbE.html#10043" class="Bound">Δ</a>
<a id="10123" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="10125" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a>       <a id="10133" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10135" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>
<a id="10137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10138" href="NbE.html#10138" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10140" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10142" href="NbE.html#10142" class="Bound">s</a><a id="10143" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10145" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a> <a id="10147" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10149" href="NbE.html#10138" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10151" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a> <a id="10153" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10155" href="NbE.html#10142" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="10157" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10159" href="NbE.html#9105" class="Function">ren-incr</a> <a id="10168" href="NbE.html#8397" class="Function Operator">]ᵣ</a>

<a id="10172" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="10178" class="Number">6</a> <a id="10180" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">_↑</a>
</pre>
Now, we can define the application of a parallel substitution
`Γ ⊢ σ : Δ` to a term `Δ ⊢ t : T` (e.g. `t [ σ ]`)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_[_]"></a><a id="10309" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">_[_]</a> <a id="10314" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10316" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10318" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10319" href="NbE.html#10319" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10321" href="NbE.html#10321" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="10323" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10325" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="10328" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10330" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10331" href="NbE.html#10331" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="10333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10335" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="10339" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="10346" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10348" href="NbE.html#10321" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="10350" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="10352" href="NbE.html#10331" class="Bound">T</a>
     <a id="10359" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10361" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="10365" href="NbE.html#10319" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10367" href="NbE.html#10321" class="Bound">Δ</a>
       <a id="10376" class="Comment">-------</a>
     <a id="10389" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10391" href="NbE.html#10319" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10393" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="10395" href="NbE.html#10331" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="10397" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="10402" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10404" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10406" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10408" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10410" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>
<a id="10415" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="10419" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10421" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10423" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10425" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10427" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a>
<a id="10431" href="NbE.html#4199" class="InductiveConstructor">rec</a> <a id="10435" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10437" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10439" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10441" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10443" href="NbE.html#4199" class="InductiveConstructor">rec</a>
<a id="10447" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10449" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="10452" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10454" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10456" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10458" href="NbE.html#10458" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10460" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10462" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10464" href="NbE.html#10458" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="10466" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10468" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="10471" href="NbE.html#10471" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10473" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10475" href="NbE.html#10475" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10477" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10479" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10481" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10483" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10485" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10487" href="NbE.html#10471" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10489" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10491" href="NbE.html#10475" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10493" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a>
<a id="10495" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10496" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10498" href="NbE.html#10498" class="Bound">t</a><a id="10499" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10501" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10503" href="NbE.html#10503" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10505" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10507" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10509" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10511" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10512" href="NbE.html#10498" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="10514" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10516" href="NbE.html#10503" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10518" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a> <a id="10520" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10522" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10524" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="10527" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="10528" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="10530" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10531" href="NbE.html#10531" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="10533" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10535" href="NbE.html#10535" class="Bound">s</a><a id="10536" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10538" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10540" href="NbE.html#10540" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10542" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10544" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10546" href="NbE.html#10531" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="10548" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10550" href="NbE.html#10540" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10552" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="10554" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10556" href="NbE.html#10535" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="10558" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10560" href="NbE.html#10540" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10562" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a>

<a id="10565" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="10571" class="Number">8</a> <a id="10573" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">_[_]</a>
</pre>
Substitutions can also be composed, by applying
a substitution `Γ₁ ⊢ τ : Ctx₂` to every term in a
substitution `Γ₂ ⊢ σ : Ctx₃`
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_∘_"></a><a id="10718" href="NbE.html#10718" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="10722" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10724" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10726" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10727" href="NbE.html#10727" class="Bound">Γ₁</a> <a id="10730" href="NbE.html#10730" class="Bound">Γ₂</a> <a id="10733" href="NbE.html#10733" class="Bound">Γ₃</a> <a id="10736" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10738" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="10741" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10745" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="10749" href="NbE.html#10730" class="Bound">Γ₂</a> <a id="10752" href="NbE.html#10733" class="Bound">Γ₃</a> <a id="10755" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10757" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="10761" href="NbE.html#10727" class="Bound">Γ₁</a> <a id="10764" href="NbE.html#10730" class="Bound">Γ₂</a> <a id="10767" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10769" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="10773" href="NbE.html#10727" class="Bound">Γ₁</a> <a id="10776" href="NbE.html#10733" class="Bound">Γ₃</a>
<a id="10779" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>       <a id="10787" href="NbE.html#10718" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10789" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10791" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10793" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>
<a id="10795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10796" href="NbE.html#10796" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10798" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10800" href="NbE.html#10800" class="Bound">s</a><a id="10801" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10803" href="NbE.html#10718" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10805" href="NbE.html#10805" class="Bound">τ</a> <a id="10807" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10810" href="NbE.html#10796" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="10812" href="NbE.html#10718" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10814" href="NbE.html#10805" class="Bound">τ</a><a id="10815" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10817" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10819" href="NbE.html#10800" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="10821" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="10823" href="NbE.html#10805" class="Bound">τ</a> <a id="10825" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a>
</pre>
We will want a weakening substitution, that allows us
to weaken a well typed term in Γ to a context Γ′ that
extends Γ.

Really, this substitution is the renaming substitution
between extended contexts
<pre class="Agda"><a id="weaken"></a><a id="11041" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="11048" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11050" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11052" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11053" href="NbE.html#11053" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="11056" href="NbE.html#11056" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11058" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11060" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="11063" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="11072" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11074" href="NbE.html#11053" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="11077" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="11079" href="NbE.html#11056" class="Bound">Γ</a>
         <a id="11090" class="Comment">--------</a>
       <a id="11106" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11108" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="11112" href="NbE.html#11053" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="11115" href="NbE.html#11056" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="11117" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="11124" href="NbE.html#11124" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="11127" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11129" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="11139" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11140" href="NbE.html#9364" class="Function">ren-≤</a> <a id="11146" href="NbE.html#11124" class="Bound">pf</a><a id="11148" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
For convenience, we will also want some shorthand for
applying a weakening substitution to a term
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_≤⊢_"></a><a id="11261" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">_≤⊢_</a> <a id="11266" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11268" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11270" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11271" href="NbE.html#11271" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="11274" href="NbE.html#11274" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11276" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11278" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="11281" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11283" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11284" href="NbE.html#11284" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="11286" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11288" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="11292" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11294" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11296" href="NbE.html#11271" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="11299" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="11301" href="NbE.html#11274" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11303" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11305" href="NbE.html#11274" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11307" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="11309" href="NbE.html#11284" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="11311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11313" href="NbE.html#11271" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="11316" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="11318" href="NbE.html#11284" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="11320" href="NbE.html#11320" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="11323" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="11326" href="NbE.html#11326" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="11328" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11330" href="NbE.html#11326" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="11332" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="11334" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="11341" href="NbE.html#11320" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="11344" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a>

<a id="11347" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="11354" class="Number">5</a> <a id="11356" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">_≤⊢_</a>
</pre>
Additionally, we define an identity and incrementing
parallel substitution, which are simply the identity and
incrementing renaming substitutions
<pre class="Agda"><a id="subst-id"></a><a id="11520" href="NbE.html#11520" class="Function">subst-id</a> <a id="11529" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11531" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11533" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11534" href="NbE.html#11534" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11536" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11538" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="11541" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11543" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11545" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="11549" href="NbE.html#11534" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11551" href="NbE.html#11534" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="11553" href="NbE.html#11520" class="Function">subst-id</a> <a id="11562" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11564" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="11574" href="NbE.html#9021" class="Function">ren-id</a>

<a id="subst-incr"></a><a id="11582" href="NbE.html#11582" class="Function">subst-incr</a> <a id="11593" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11595" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11598" href="NbE.html#11598" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11602" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="11605" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11607" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11608" href="NbE.html#11608" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="11610" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11612" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="11616" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11618" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11620" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="11624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11625" href="NbE.html#11598" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11627" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11629" href="NbE.html#11608" class="Bound">T</a><a id="11630" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11632" href="NbE.html#11598" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="11634" href="NbE.html#11582" class="Function">subst-incr</a> <a id="11645" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11647" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="11657" href="NbE.html#9105" class="Function">ren-incr</a>
</pre>
The incrementing substitution will be used to establish
η-equivalence, we will also benfit from some shorthand for
its application to a term
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_↑⊢_"></a><a id="11820" href="NbE.html#11820" class="Function Operator">_↑⊢_</a> <a id="11825" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11827" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11829" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11830" href="NbE.html#11830" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11832" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11834" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="11837" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11839" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11840" href="NbE.html#11840" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="11842" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11844" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="11848" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11850" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11852" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11853" href="NbE.html#11853" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="11855" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11857" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="11861" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11863" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11865" href="NbE.html#11830" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11867" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="11869" href="NbE.html#11840" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="11871" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11873" href="NbE.html#11830" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="11875" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11877" href="NbE.html#11853" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="11879" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="11881" href="NbE.html#11840" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="11883" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="11885" href="NbE.html#11820" class="Function Operator">↑⊢</a> <a id="11888" href="NbE.html#11888" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="11890" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11892" href="NbE.html#11888" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="11894" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="11896" href="NbE.html#11582" class="Function">subst-incr</a> <a id="11907" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a>

<a id="11910" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="11917" class="Number">5</a> <a id="11919" href="NbE.html#11820" class="Function Operator">_↑⊢_</a>
</pre>
To establish β-equivalence, we define an operation for
substituting the first free variable in a term `Γ , x:S ⊢ t : T`
with a term `Γ ⊢ s : S` (i.e. `t [ s / x ]`), which is really
shorthand for `t [ id , s / x ]`
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_[_/x]"></a><a id="12152" href="NbE.html#12152" class="Function Operator">_[_/x]</a> <a id="12159" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12161" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12163" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12164" href="NbE.html#12164" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12166" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12168" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="12171" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12173" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12174" href="NbE.html#12174" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="12176" href="NbE.html#12176" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="12178" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12180" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="12184" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="12188" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12190" href="NbE.html#12164" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12192" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12194" href="NbE.html#12176" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="12196" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12198" href="NbE.html#12174" class="Bound">S</a>
  <a id="12202" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12204" href="NbE.html#12164" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12206" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12208" href="NbE.html#12176" class="Bound">T</a>
    <a id="12214" class="Comment">---------</a>
  <a id="12226" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12228" href="NbE.html#12164" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12230" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12232" href="NbE.html#12174" class="Bound">S</a>
<a id="12234" href="NbE.html#12234" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="12236" href="NbE.html#12152" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="12238" href="NbE.html#12238" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="12240" href="NbE.html#12152" class="Function Operator">/x]</a> <a id="12244" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="12247" href="NbE.html#12234" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="12249" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="12251" href="NbE.html#11520" class="Function">subst-id</a> <a id="12260" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12262" href="NbE.html#12238" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="12264" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a>

<a id="12267" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="12273" class="Number">8</a> <a id="12275" href="NbE.html#12152" class="Function Operator">_[_/x]</a>
</pre>
With these defined, we can introduce a new relation between two
terms: definitional equality. In the thesis, this is
written as `Γ ⊢ t = t′ : T`, we will use t == t′ in Agda

The relation is written such that the definitional equality
of two terms implies the equality of their interpretations
(`Γ ⊢ t = t′ : T` iff `⟦ t ⟧ = ⟦ t′ ⟧`); it is the extension of
Βη-equivalence for System T suggested earlier

We will use this relation to prove the soundness property
of preservation of meaning for NbE (i.e. `⟦ nf(t) ⟧ = ⟦ t ⟧`)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="12820" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_==_"></a><a id="12825" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a> <a id="12830" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12832" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12834" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12835" href="NbE.html#12835" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12837" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12839" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="12842" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12844" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12845" href="NbE.html#12845" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="12847" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12849" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="12853" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12855" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12857" href="NbE.html#12835" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12859" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12861" href="NbE.html#12845" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="12863" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12865" href="NbE.html#12835" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="12867" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="12869" href="NbE.html#12845" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="12871" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12873" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="12877" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12886" class="Comment">-- Computation rules</a>

          <a id="14422" class="Comment">-------</a>
