  <a id="_==_.trans"></a><a id="14451" href="NbE.html#14451" class="InductiveConstructor">trans</a> <a id="14457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14459" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14462" href="NbE.html#14462" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14464" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14466" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="14469" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14471" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14472" href="NbE.html#14472" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="14474" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14476" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="14480" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14482" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14483" href="NbE.html#14483" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="14486" href="NbE.html#14486" class="Bound">t₂</a> <a id="14489" href="NbE.html#14489" class="Bound">t₃</a> <a id="14492" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14494" href="NbE.html#14462" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14496" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="14498" href="NbE.html#14472" class="Bound">T</a><a id="14499" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="14511" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14513" href="NbE.html#14483" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="14516" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14519" href="NbE.html#14486" class="Bound">t₂</a>
          <a id="14532" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14534" href="NbE.html#14486" class="Bound">t₂</a> <a id="14537" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14540" href="NbE.html#14489" class="Bound">t₃</a>
            <a id="14555" class="Comment">--------</a>
          <a id="14574" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14576" href="NbE.html#14483" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="14579" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14582" href="NbE.html#14489" class="Bound">t₃</a>

<a id="14586" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="14592" class="Number">3</a> <a id="14594" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">_==_</a>
</pre>
For the clarity of some of our proofs, it will also be helpful to
have the ability to use equational reasoning with respect to
definitional equality.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="14762" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="==-Reasoning"></a><a id="14769" href="NbE.html#14769" class="Module">==-Reasoning</a> <a id="14782" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14790" class="Keyword">infix</a>  <a id="14797" class="Number">1</a> <a id="14799" href="NbE.html#14842" class="Function Operator">begin_</a>
  <a id="14808" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="14815" class="Number">2</a> <a id="14817" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">_==⟨_⟩_</a>
  <a id="14827" class="Keyword">infix</a>  <a id="14834" class="Number">3</a> <a id="14836" href="NbE.html#15125" class="Function Operator">_∎</a>

  <a id="==-Reasoning.begin_"></a><a id="14842" href="NbE.html#14842" class="Function Operator">begin_</a> <a id="14849" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14851" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14853" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14854" href="NbE.html#14854" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14856" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14858" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="14861" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14863" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14864" href="NbE.html#14864" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="14866" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14868" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="14872" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14874" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14875" href="NbE.html#14875" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="14877" href="NbE.html#14877" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="14880" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14882" href="NbE.html#14854" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14884" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="14886" href="NbE.html#14864" class="Bound">T</a><a id="14887" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="14893" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14895" href="NbE.html#14875" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="14897" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14900" href="NbE.html#14877" class="Bound">t′</a>
      <a id="14909" class="Comment">---------</a>
    <a id="14923" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14925" href="NbE.html#14875" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="14927" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14930" href="NbE.html#14877" class="Bound">t′</a>
  <a id="14935" href="NbE.html#14842" class="Function Operator">begin</a> <a id="14941" href="NbE.html#14941" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="14944" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14946" href="NbE.html#14941" class="Bound">pf</a>

  <a id="==-Reasoning._==⟨_⟩_"></a><a id="14952" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">_==⟨_⟩_</a> <a id="14960" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14962" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14964" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14965" href="NbE.html#14965" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14967" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14969" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="14972" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14974" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14975" href="NbE.html#14975" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="14977" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14979" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="14983" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14985" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14986" href="NbE.html#14986" class="Bound">t₂</a> <a id="14989" href="NbE.html#14989" class="Bound">t₃</a> <a id="14992" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14994" href="NbE.html#14965" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="14996" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="14998" href="NbE.html#14975" class="Bound">T</a><a id="14999" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="15005" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15007" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15008" href="NbE.html#15008" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="15011" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15013" href="NbE.html#14965" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="15015" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="15017" href="NbE.html#14975" class="Bound">T</a><a id="15018" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="15024" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15026" href="NbE.html#15008" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="15029" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="15032" href="NbE.html#14986" class="Bound">t₂</a>
    <a id="15039" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15041" href="NbE.html#14986" class="Bound">t₂</a> <a id="15044" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="15047" href="NbE.html#14989" class="Bound">t₃</a>
      <a id="15056" class="Comment">-----</a>
    <a id="15066" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15068" href="NbE.html#15008" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="15071" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="15074" href="NbE.html#14989" class="Bound">t₃</a>
  <a id="15079" href="NbE.html#15079" class="Bound">t₁</a> <a id="15082" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="15086" href="NbE.html#15086" class="Bound">t₁≡t₂</a> <a id="15092" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15094" href="NbE.html#15094" class="Bound">t₂≡t₃</a>  <a id="15101" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="15104" href="NbE.html#14451" class="InductiveConstructor">trans</a> <a id="15110" href="NbE.html#15086" class="Bound">t₁≡t₂</a> <a id="15116" href="NbE.html#15094" class="Bound">t₂≡t₃</a>

  <a id="==-Reasoning._∎"></a><a id="15125" href="NbE.html#15125" class="Function Operator">_∎</a> <a id="15128" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15130" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15132" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15133" href="NbE.html#15133" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="15135" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15137" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="15140" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15142" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15143" href="NbE.html#15143" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="15145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15147" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="15151" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15153" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15155" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15156" href="NbE.html#15156" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="15158" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15160" href="NbE.html#15133" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="15162" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="15164" href="NbE.html#15143" class="Bound">T</a><a id="15165" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="15173" class="Comment">-----</a>
    <a id="15183" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15185" href="NbE.html#15156" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="15187" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="15190" href="NbE.html#15156" class="Bound">t</a>
  <a id="15194" href="NbE.html#15194" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="15196" href="NbE.html#15125" class="Function Operator">∎</a>  <a id="15199" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="15202" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

<a id="15208" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15213" href="NbE.html#14769" class="Module">==-Reasoning</a> <a id="15226" class="Keyword">public</a>
</pre>
Now, we are ready to start defining the algorithm for normalization by
evaluation. Normalization by evaluation is the process of obtaining the normal
form of a term by evaluating it in a meta language (in our case, Agda).

Evaluating terms in System T in our meta language will require defining the interpretations of its types, contexts, and terms.

We use the following record to represent interpretations of types and contexts in System T, indicated by ⟦_⟧.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="15707" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Interpretation"></a><a id="15714" href="NbE.html#15714" class="Record">Interpretation</a> <a id="15729" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15730" href="NbE.html#15730" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="15732" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15734" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a><a id="15737" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15741" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set₁</a> <a id="15746" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="15754" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="Interpretation.⟦_⟧"></a><a id="15764" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦_⟧</a> <a id="15768" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15770" href="NbE.html#15730" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="15772" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15774" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>

<a id="15779" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15784" href="NbE.html#15714" class="Module">Interpretation</a> <a id="15799" class="Symbol">{{...}}</a> <a id="15807" class="Keyword">public</a>
</pre>
The thesis first introduces a more traditional interpretation of these,
but these definitions will need to be updated in our final implementation
of the NbE algorithm.

For types, we can interpret naturals in System T as ℕ, and functions in
System T as Agda functions, defined inductively on their types.

    ⟦ nat ⟧ = ℕ
    ⟦ S ⇒ T ⟧ = ⟦ S ⟧ → ⟦ T ⟧

An empty context is interpreted as the unit type, and an extension to
a context is defined inductively, with the extension itself being the
interpretation of the type the context is extended with.

    ⟦ ∅ ⟧ = ⊤
    ⟦ Γ , S ⟧ = ⟦ Γ ⟧ × ⟦ S ⟧

From now on, we will use the metavariable ρ is used to represent elements of ⟦ Γ ⟧ for a context Γ.

The interpretation of a variable expects the interpretation
of a context, and is essentially a lookup:

    ⟦ Γ ∋ x:T ⟧ (ρ ∈ ⟦Γ⟧) ∈ ⟦ T ⟧
    ⟦ Γ , T ∋ x:T ⟧ (ρ , a) = a
    ⟦ Γ , y:S ∋ x:T ⟧ (ρ , _) = ⟦ Γ ∋ x:T ⟧ ρ

The interpretation of a typed term expects the interpretation
of a context as well. It is more involed, so we only include
the rule for variables and abstractions:

    ⟦ Γ ⊢ t : T ⟧ (ρ ∈ ⟦Γ⟧) = ⟦ T ⟧
    ⟦ Γ ⊢ x : T ⟧ ρ = ⟦ Γ ∋ x:T ⟧ ρ
    ⟦ Γ ⊢ λx . t : S ⇒ T ⟧ ρ  a  = ⟦ Γ , x:S ⊢ t : T ⟧ (ρ , a)

As our final definition of interpretation will change, this is
only a rough sketch, but gives an idea of how we can evaluate terms
in Agda. For now, we only include the concrete interpretation of
a context Γ (generalized over any interpretation of types), as it will
remain unchanged.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="17328" class="Keyword">instance</a>
    <a id="17341" class="Comment">-- We only include the concrete interpretation of a</a>
    <a id="17397" class="Comment">-- context Γ, generalized over any interpretation of</a>
    <a id="17454" class="Comment">-- types, to be used with the actual interpretation</a>
    <a id="17510" class="Comment">-- defined later</a>
    <a id="⟦Γ⟧"></a><a id="17531" href="NbE.html#17531" class="Function">⟦Γ⟧</a> <a id="17535" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17537" class="Symbol">{{</a><a id="17539" href="NbE.html#17539" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="17541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17543" href="NbE.html#15714" class="Record">Interpretation</a> <a id="17558" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="17562" class="Symbol">}}</a> <a id="17565" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17567" href="NbE.html#15714" class="Record">Interpretation</a> <a id="17582" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a>
    <a id="17590" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">Interpretation.⟦</a> <a id="17607" href="NbE.html#17531" class="Function">⟦Γ⟧</a> <a id="17611" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="17613" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="17615" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17617" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#164" class="Record">⊤</a>
    <a id="17623" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">Interpretation.⟦</a> <a id="17640" href="NbE.html#17531" class="Function">⟦Γ⟧</a> <a id="17644" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="17646" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17647" href="NbE.html#17647" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="17649" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="17651" href="NbE.html#17651" class="Bound">T</a><a id="17652" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17654" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17656" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="17658" href="NbE.html#17647" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="17660" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="17662" href="Data.Product.html#1167" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="17664" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="17666" href="NbE.html#17651" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="17668" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a>
</pre>
To motivate our algorithm, first we recognize that normalization by evaluation is,
intuitively, the evaulation of an expression with unknowns (e.g. variables) to
another, possibly simplified, expression with unknowns.

Because of this, we arrive at the first change to our interpretation of terms.
The interpretation of the base type nat is now terms of type nat in their
normal form -- after all, a variable of type nat is "blocked" and cannot be
evaluated any further. In other words, we now have:

    ⟦ nat ⟧ = terms of type nat in their normal form

From now on, normalized terms with unknowns will be referred to as neutral terms
(indicated by the metavariable 𝓊 for "unknown"), and normalized terms in general
will be referred to as normal terms (indicated by the metavariable 𝓋 for "value").

Additionally, while evaluation gives us the ability to normalize terms,
it also transforms them into our meta language. We want a way to return
to System T, which will be a function we will refer to as reification.
We will refer to its opposite, e.g. the transformation of a term in System T
into our meta language, as reflection.

The normal form of a typed term t in context Γ will be obtained by using
reflection and reification together. The following steps make up a sketch
of the algorithm:

  1) reflect the variables of the context Γ
     (all of which are neutral terms)
  2) interpret the value of the term using the environment
     of reflected variables
  3) "reify" the interpreted value of the term (i.e. returning
     it to a term in normal form)

Before we can actually define the algorithm, we need to formally introduce
normal and neutral terms in Agda, which we define mutually. The constructors
for these represent the different types of normal terms, and they are parametrized
by the terms themselves.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="19510" class="Comment">-- Neutral terms</a>
<a id="19527" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Ne"></a><a id="19532" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="19535" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19536" href="NbE.html#19536" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="19538" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19540" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="19544" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19546" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19547" href="NbE.html#19547" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19551" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="19554" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19556" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19558" href="NbE.html#19547" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19560" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19562" href="NbE.html#19536" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="19564" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19566" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
<a id="19570" class="Comment">-- Normal Terms</a>
<a id="19586" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Nf"></a><a id="19591" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="19594" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19597" href="NbE.html#19597" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="19599" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19601" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="19605" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19607" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19610" href="NbE.html#19610" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19612" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19614" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="19617" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19619" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19621" href="NbE.html#19610" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19623" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19625" href="NbE.html#19597" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="19627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19629" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
</pre>
Neutral terms are normal terms in their blocked form. Variables are the "base
case" for blocked terms. Application on an unknown function to a normal term is
also blocked, as is recursion on an unknown natural.
blocked terms.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="19872" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="19877" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="19880" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="19882" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19884" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Ne.ne-var"></a><a id="19892" href="NbE.html#19892" class="InductiveConstructor">ne-var</a> <a id="19899" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19901" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19902" href="NbE.html#19902" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19904" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19906" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19908" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="19910" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a><a id="19911" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="19924" class="Comment">------------</a>
         <a id="19946" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19948" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="19951" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="19953" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19956" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="19958" href="NbE.html#19902" class="Bound">x</a><a id="19959" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="Ne.ne-app"></a><a id="19964" href="NbE.html#19964" class="InductiveConstructor">ne-app</a> <a id="19971" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19973" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19975" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19976" href="NbE.html#19976" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="19978" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19980" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="19984" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19986" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19987" href="NbE.html#19987" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="19989" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19991" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19993" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19995" href="NbE.html#19976" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="19997" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="19999" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20000" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20002" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20003" href="NbE.html#20003" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="20005" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20007" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20009" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20011" href="NbE.html#19976" class="Bound">S</a><a id="20012" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="20023" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20025" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="20028" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20029" href="NbE.html#19976" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="20031" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="20033" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20034" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20036" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20038" href="NbE.html#19987" class="Bound">𝓊</a>
         <a id="20049" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20051" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20054" href="NbE.html#19976" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="20056" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20058" href="NbE.html#20003" class="Bound">𝓋</a>
           <a id="20071" class="Comment">--------------</a>
         <a id="20095" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20097" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="20100" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20102" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20105" href="NbE.html#19987" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="20107" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="20109" href="NbE.html#20003" class="Bound">𝓋</a><a id="20110" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="Ne.ne-rec"></a><a id="20115" href="NbE.html#20115" class="InductiveConstructor">ne-rec</a> <a id="20122" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20124" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20125" href="NbE.html#20125" class="Bound">𝓋z</a> <a id="20128" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20130" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20132" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20134" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20135" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20137" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20138" href="NbE.html#20138" class="Bound">𝓋s</a> <a id="20141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20143" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20145" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20147" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="20151" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="20153" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20155" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="20157" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20158" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20160" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20161" href="NbE.html#20161" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="20163" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20165" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20167" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20169" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="20172" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="20183" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20185" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20188" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20190" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20192" href="NbE.html#20125" class="Bound">𝓋z</a>
         <a id="20204" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20206" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20209" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20210" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="20214" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="20216" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20218" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="20220" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20221" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20223" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20225" href="NbE.html#20138" class="Bound">𝓋s</a>
         <a id="20237" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20239" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="20242" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="20246" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20248" href="NbE.html#20161" class="Bound">𝓊</a>
           <a id="20261" class="Comment">--------------------------</a>
         <a id="20297" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20299" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="20302" href="NbE.html#19880" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20304" href="NbE.html#19882" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20306" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20307" href="NbE.html#4199" class="InductiveConstructor">rec</a> <a id="20311" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="20313" href="NbE.html#20125" class="Bound">𝓋z</a> <a id="20316" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="20318" href="NbE.html#20138" class="Bound">𝓋s</a> <a id="20321" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="20323" href="NbE.html#20161" class="Bound">𝓊</a><a id="20324" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Normal terms are terms in their normal form. `zero`, and `suc` applied to a
normal term are normalized naturals. An abstraction whose body is normalized
is itself normalized, as is any neutral term.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="20538" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="20543" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20546" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Nf.nf-zero"></a><a id="20554" href="NbE.html#20554" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-zero</a> <a id="20562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20564" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20566" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20567" href="NbE.html#20567" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20569" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20571" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="20574" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20576" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20578" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20581" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="20585" href="NbE.html#20567" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20587" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>

  <a id="Nf.nf-suc"></a><a id="20595" href="NbE.html#20595" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-suc</a> <a id="20602" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20604" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20606" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20607" href="NbE.html#20607" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20609" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20611" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="20614" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20616" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20617" href="NbE.html#20617" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="20619" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20621" href="NbE.html#20607" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20623" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20625" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="20628" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="20639" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20641" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20644" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="20648" href="NbE.html#20607" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20650" href="NbE.html#20617" class="Bound">𝓋</a>
           <a id="20663" class="Comment">------------------</a>
         <a id="20691" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20693" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20696" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="20700" href="NbE.html#20607" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20702" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20703" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="20707" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="20709" href="NbE.html#20617" class="Bound">𝓋</a><a id="20710" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="Nf.nf-abs"></a><a id="20715" href="NbE.html#20715" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-abs</a> <a id="20722" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20724" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20726" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20727" href="NbE.html#20727" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="20729" href="NbE.html#20729" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20733" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="20737" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20739" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20740" href="NbE.html#20740" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20742" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20744" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="20747" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20749" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20750" href="NbE.html#20750" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="20752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20754" href="NbE.html#20740" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20756" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20758" href="NbE.html#20727" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="20760" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20762" href="NbE.html#20729" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20763" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="20774" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20776" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20779" href="NbE.html#20729" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20781" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20782" href="NbE.html#20740" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20784" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="20786" href="NbE.html#20727" class="Bound">S</a><a id="20787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20789" href="NbE.html#20750" class="Bound">𝓋</a>
           <a id="20802" class="Comment">------------------</a>
         <a id="20830" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20832" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20835" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20836" href="NbE.html#20727" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="20838" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="20840" href="NbE.html#20729" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20841" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20843" href="NbE.html#20740" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20845" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20846" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="20848" href="NbE.html#20750" class="Bound">𝓋</a><a id="20849" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="Nf.nf-neutral"></a><a id="20854" href="NbE.html#20854" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-neutral</a> <a id="20865" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20867" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20869" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20870" href="NbE.html#20870" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20872" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20874" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="20878" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20880" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20881" href="NbE.html#20881" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20883" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20885" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="20888" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20890" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20891" href="NbE.html#20891" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="20893" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20895" href="NbE.html#20881" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20897" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20899" href="NbE.html#20870" class="Bound">T</a><a id="20900" class="Symbol">}</a>
             <a id="20915" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20917" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="20920" href="NbE.html#20870" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20922" href="NbE.html#20881" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20924" href="NbE.html#20891" class="Bound">𝓊</a>
               <a id="20941" class="Comment">--------</a>
             <a id="20963" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20965" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="20968" href="NbE.html#20870" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="20970" href="NbE.html#20881" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20972" href="NbE.html#20891" class="Bound">𝓊</a>
</pre>
With these defined, we can give a more formal (but still not final) sketch
of our algorithm:

    ⟦ nat ⟧ = Nf nat

    ↑ᵀ ∈ Ne T → ⟦ T ⟧
    ↑ⁿᵃᵗ 𝓊 = 𝓊
    ↑ˢ⃗ᵗ 𝓊 (a ∈ ⟦ S ⟧) = ↑ᵀ (𝓊 𝓋) , 𝓋 = ↓ˢ a
    
    ↓ᵀ ∈ ⟦ T ⟧ → Nf T
    ↓ⁿᵃᵗ 𝓋 = 𝓋
    ↓ˢ⃗ᵗ f = λx. ↓ᵀ (f(a)) , where a = ↑ᵀ x and x is "fresh"
    
    ↑ᶜᵗˣ ∈ ⟦ Γ ⟧
    ↑∅ = tt
    ↑ᶜᵗˣ,x:S = ↑ᶜᵗˣ , ↑ˢ x
    
    nf(t) = ↓ᵀ (⟦ t ⟧ ↑ᶜᵗˣ)

The algorithm takes a term, evaluates it in an environment of reflected
variables, and then reifies it back to System T. However, this sketch
has an immediate issue to figure out -- how to determine the freshness
condition for the variable x used when reifying at function type.

As we are using de Brujin indices, this has a simple solution: just extend
the context. However, there is no context anywhere in our definition
of reification, so what context do we extend with the fresh variable?
This is actually intentional, because of an issue that is more subtle:
after we reflect the variable, it may later be reified in a different
context than it was created.

To address this, we introduce liftable terms. These are terms that are
generalized over contexts, and can be applied to any context Γ.

An effect of this is that it could be that the resulting term is not
well defined. In fact, it will be the case that liftable neutral terms can
only be applied to extensions of the context under which they were created.
Because of this, liftable neutrals will need to return a placeholder value (tt)
for some contexts.

We append the up arrow ↑ for the liftable version of a System T construct, and
use 𝓋̂ and 𝓊̂ as the metavariables for liftable normal terms and neutral terms
respectively.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="22676" class="Comment">-- Liftable neutral term</a>
<a id="Ne↑"></a><a id="22701" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="22705" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22707" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="22712" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22714" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
<a id="22718" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="22722" href="NbE.html#22722" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="22724" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22726" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22728" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22729" href="NbE.html#22729" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="22731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22733" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="22736" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22738" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22740" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="22743" href="NbE.html#22743" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="22745" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">]</a> <a id="22747" href="NbE.html#19532" class="Datatype">Ne</a> <a id="22750" href="NbE.html#22722" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="22752" href="NbE.html#22729" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="22754" href="NbE.html#22743" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="22756" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#734" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="22758" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#164" class="Record">⊤</a>

<a id="22761" class="Comment">-- Liftable normal term</a>
<a id="Nf↑"></a><a id="22785" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="22789" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22791" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="22796" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22798" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
<a id="22802" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="22806" href="NbE.html#22806" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="22808" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22810" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22812" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22813" href="NbE.html#22813" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="22815" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22817" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="22820" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22822" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22824" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="22827" href="NbE.html#22827" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="22829" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">]</a> <a id="22831" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="22834" href="NbE.html#22806" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="22836" href="NbE.html#22813" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="22838" href="NbE.html#22827" class="Bound">t</a>
</pre>
Application of liftable terms is overloaded, i.e. (𝓊̂ 𝓋̂)(Γ) = 𝓊̂(Γ)𝓋̂(Γ)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_·↑_"></a><a id="22927" href="NbE.html#22927" class="Function Operator">_·↑_</a> <a id="22932" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22934" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22936" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22937" href="NbE.html#22937" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="22939" href="NbE.html#22939" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="22941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22943" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="22947" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22949" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22951" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="22955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22956" href="NbE.html#22937" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="22958" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="22960" href="NbE.html#22939" class="Bound">T</a><a id="22961" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22963" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="22966" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="22970" href="NbE.html#22937" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="22972" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22974" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="22978" href="NbE.html#22939" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="22980" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22981" href="NbE.html#22981" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="22984" href="NbE.html#22927" class="Function Operator">·↑</a> <a id="22987" href="NbE.html#22987" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a><a id="22989" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22991" href="NbE.html#22991" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="22993" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="22998" href="NbE.html#22981" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="23001" href="NbE.html#22991" class="Bound">Γ</a>               <a id="23017" class="Symbol">|</a>          <a id="23028" href="NbE.html#22987" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a> <a id="23031" href="NbE.html#22991" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="23033" class="Symbol">...</a>           <a id="23047" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="23049" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="23054" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="23056" href="NbE.html#23056" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="23058" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23060" href="NbE.html#23060" class="Bound">pf-𝓊</a> <a id="23065" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="23067" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="23069" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="23071" href="NbE.html#23071" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="23073" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23075" href="NbE.html#23075" class="Bound">pf-𝓋</a> <a id="23080" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="23082" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="23090" class="Comment">-- Note that we need to provide proof</a>
      <a id="23134" class="Comment">-- that our resulting lifted term is</a>
      <a id="23177" class="Comment">-- a neutral term as well</a>
      <a id="23209" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="23214" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="23216" href="NbE.html#23056" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="23218" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="23220" href="NbE.html#23071" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="23222" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23224" href="NbE.html#19964" class="InductiveConstructor">ne-app</a> <a id="23231" href="NbE.html#23060" class="Bound">pf-𝓊</a> <a id="23236" href="NbE.html#23075" class="Bound">pf-𝓋</a> <a id="23241" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="23243" class="Symbol">...</a>           <a id="23257" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="23259" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#809" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="23264" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>           <a id="23277" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="23279" class="Symbol">_</a>            <a id="23292" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23294" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#809" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="23299" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
</pre>
Since normalization by evaluation will need to be
over liftable terms, the concrete interpretation of
the base type nat will in the end be naturals with embedded liftable
neutrals, which we can now finally define in Agda, along with the
interpretation of types.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="23577" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ̂"></a><a id="23582" href="NbE.html#23582" class="Datatype">ℕ̂</a> <a id="23585" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23587" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a> <a id="23591" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ̂.zero"></a><a id="23599" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="23604" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23606" href="NbE.html#23582" class="Datatype">ℕ̂</a>
  <a id="ℕ̂.suc"></a><a id="23611" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="23615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23617" href="NbE.html#23582" class="Datatype">ℕ̂</a> <a id="23620" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23622" href="NbE.html#23582" class="Datatype">ℕ̂</a>
  <a id="ℕ̂.ne"></a><a id="23627" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="23630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23632" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="23636" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="23640" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23642" href="NbE.html#23582" class="Datatype">ℕ̂</a>

<a id="23646" class="Keyword">instance</a>
  <a id="⟦Type⟧"></a><a id="23657" href="NbE.html#23657" class="Function">⟦Type⟧</a> <a id="23664" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23666" href="NbE.html#15714" class="Record">Interpretation</a> <a id="23681" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a>
  <a id="23688" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">Interpretation.⟦</a> <a id="23705" href="NbE.html#23657" class="Function">⟦Type⟧</a> <a id="23712" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="23714" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="23718" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23720" href="NbE.html#23582" class="Datatype">ℕ̂</a>
  <a id="23725" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">Interpretation.⟦</a> <a id="23742" href="NbE.html#23657" class="Function">⟦Type⟧</a> <a id="23749" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="23751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23752" href="NbE.html#23752" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="23754" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="23756" href="NbE.html#23756" class="Bound">T</a><a id="23757" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23759" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23761" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="23763" href="NbE.html#23752" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="23765" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="23767" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23769" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="23771" href="NbE.html#23756" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="23773" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a>
</pre>
With this, we begin the most important part
of normalization by evaluation, the reflection
and reification functions. These are mutually
recursive, and will be defined inductively
on the type T

<pre class="Agda"><a id="23983" class="Comment">-- Reflection of neutral terms of type T into</a>
<a id="24029" class="Comment">-- semantic objects in ⟦T⟧</a>
<a id="↑ᵀ"></a><a id="24056" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="24059" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24061" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24062" href="NbE.html#24062" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="24064" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24066" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="24070" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24072" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24074" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="24078" href="NbE.html#24062" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="24080" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24082" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="24084" href="NbE.html#24062" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="24086" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a>

<a id="24089" class="Comment">-- Reification of semantic objects in ⟦T⟧ into</a>
<a id="24136" class="Comment">-- normal terms of type T</a>
<a id="↓ᵀ"></a><a id="24162" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="24165" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24167" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24168" href="NbE.html#24168" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="24170" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24172" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="24176" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24178" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24180" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="24182" href="NbE.html#24168" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="24184" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="24186" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24188" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="24192" href="NbE.html#24168" class="Bound">T</a>
</pre>
As was the case in the sketch of the algorithm, the reflection
of a liftable neutral of type nat into the metalanguage (i.e. into
a term ℕ̂) is just the liftable neutral itself, embedded with the
ne constructor.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="24419" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="24422" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24423" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="24426" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24428" href="NbE.html#24428" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="24431" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24433" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="24436" href="NbE.html#24428" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a>
</pre>
As for the reflection of neutral terms of type S ⇒ T into ⟦S⟧ → ⟦T⟧,
we reify a semantic object in ⟦S⟧ and then reflect the neutral term
resulting from the application of the reified object to the original
neutral term. Here, we use the liftable application operation we
defined earlier.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="24740" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="24743" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24744" href="NbE.html#24744" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="24746" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="24748" href="NbE.html#24748" class="Bound">T</a><a id="24749" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24751" href="NbE.html#24751" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="24754" href="NbE.html#24754" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24756" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24758" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="24761" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24762" href="NbE.html#24751" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="24765" href="NbE.html#22927" class="Function Operator">·↑</a> <a id="24768" href="NbE.html#24778" class="Function">𝓋̂</a><a id="24770" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24772" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="24778" href="NbE.html#24778" class="Function">𝓋̂</a> <a id="24781" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24783" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="24786" href="NbE.html#24754" class="Bound">a</a>
</pre>
For the reification of semantic objects of type ⟦nat⟧,
which are our naturals with embedded liftable neutrals (ℕ̂),
we define the following helper function.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="↓ℕ̂"></a><a id="24958" href="NbE.html#24958" class="Function">↓ℕ̂</a> <a id="24962" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24964" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="24966" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="24970" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="24972" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24974" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="24978" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a>
<a id="24982" href="NbE.html#24958" class="Function">↓ℕ̂</a> <a id="24986" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="24991" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24993" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="24996" href="NbE.html#24996" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="24998" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25000" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="25002" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="25007" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="25009" href="NbE.html#20554" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-zero</a> <a id="25017" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a><a id="25018" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
For the successor case, we reify the successor into a liftable
successor function (suc↑) applied to the reification of the argument
to the successor function
<pre class="Agda"><a id="25191" href="NbE.html#24958" class="Function">↓ℕ̂</a> <a id="25195" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25196" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="25200" href="NbE.html#25200" class="Bound">n</a><a id="25201" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25203" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25205" href="NbE.html#25226" class="Function">suc↑</a> <a id="25210" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25211" href="NbE.html#24958" class="Function">↓ℕ̂</a> <a id="25215" href="NbE.html#25200" class="Bound">n</a><a id="25216" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25218" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="25226" href="NbE.html#25226" class="Function">suc↑</a> <a id="25231" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25233" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="25237" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="25241" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25243" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="25247" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a>
  <a id="25253" href="NbE.html#25226" class="Function">suc↑</a> <a id="25258" href="NbE.html#25258" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a> <a id="25261" href="NbE.html#25261" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="25263" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="25269" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="25273" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="25275" href="NbE.html#25275" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="25277" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="25279" href="NbE.html#25279" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="25282" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="25284" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25286" href="NbE.html#25258" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a> <a id="25289" href="NbE.html#25261" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="25291" class="Keyword">in</a>
    <a id="25298" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="25300" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="25304" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="25306" href="NbE.html#25275" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="25308" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="25310" href="NbE.html#20595" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-suc</a> <a id="25317" href="NbE.html#25279" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="25320" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>
In the case of an embedded liftable neutral, we use `zero` as a
fallback if the liftable neutral is undefined at the context.
Our proof of soundness later will be proof that this fallback is not
necessary in our algorithm.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="25558" href="NbE.html#24958" class="Function">↓ℕ̂</a> <a id="25562" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25563" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="25566" href="NbE.html#25566" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="25568" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25570" href="NbE.html#25570" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="25572" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="25577" href="NbE.html#25566" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="25580" href="NbE.html#25570" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="25582" class="Symbol">...</a>            <a id="25597" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="25599" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="25604" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="25606" href="NbE.html#25606" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="25608" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="25610" href="NbE.html#25610" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="25613" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="25615" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25617" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="25619" href="NbE.html#25606" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="25621" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="25623" href="NbE.html#20854" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-neutral</a> <a id="25634" href="NbE.html#25610" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="25637" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="25639" class="Symbol">...</a>            <a id="25654" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="25656" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#809" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="25661" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>         <a id="25672" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25674" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="25676" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="25681" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="25683" href="NbE.html#20554" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-zero</a> <a id="25691" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>
For reification at function type, we will need the following
function which creates a "fresh" variable for a context Γ.
Really, this is just the de Brujin index 0 for a context `Γ , x:S`.
This will be a liftable variable that can be used in a context
that is an extension of `Γ , x:S` (and is undefined otherwise).
<pre class="Agda"><a id="𝓍̂"></a><a id="26017" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="26020" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26022" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26023" href="NbE.html#26023" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="26025" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26027" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="26031" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26033" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26035" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a> <a id="26039" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26041" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="26045" href="NbE.html#26023" class="Bound">S</a>
<a id="26047" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="26050" href="NbE.html#26050" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="26052" href="NbE.html#26052" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26054" href="NbE.html#26054" class="Bound">Γ′</a>
  <a id="26059" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="26064" href="NbE.html#26054" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="26067" href="NbE.html#2934" class="Function Operator">≤?</a> <a id="26070" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26071" href="NbE.html#26052" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26073" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26075" href="NbE.html#26050" class="Bound">S</a><a id="26076" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="26078" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="26083" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="26085" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1685" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="26088" class="Symbol">_</a>          <a id="26099" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26101" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#809" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="26106" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
<a id="26109" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="26114" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="26116" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1648" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="26120" href="NbE.html#26120" class="Bound">pf</a>
  <a id="26125" class="Comment">-- The variable x in the extended context Γ′ can</a>
  <a id="26176" class="Comment">-- be accessed through the renaming between Γ′ and</a>
  <a id="26229" class="Comment">-- Γ , S</a>
  <a id="26240" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="26245" href="NbE.html#9364" class="Function">ren-≤</a> <a id="26251" href="NbE.html#26120" class="Bound">pf</a>
<a id="26254" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="26259" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="26261" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="26263" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26265" href="NbE.html#26265" class="Bound">x</a>         <a id="26275" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26277" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="26282" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="26284" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="26286" href="NbE.html#26265" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="26288" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26290" href="NbE.html#19892" class="InductiveConstructor">ne-var</a> <a id="26297" href="NbE.html#26265" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="26299" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>
For our reification function, we reuse ↓ℕ̂ at type nat.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="26370" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="26373" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26374" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="26377" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26379" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26381" href="NbE.html#24958" class="Function">↓ℕ̂</a>
</pre>
For the eification of semantic objects of type ⟦S → T⟧ (which are functions
of type ⟦S⟧ → ⟦T⟧), the resulting normal term is an abstraction over the
reification of the function applied to the reflection of the bound variable,
for which we use 𝓍̂
 <pre class="Agda"><a id="26645" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="26648" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26649" href="NbE.html#26649" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="26651" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="26653" href="NbE.html#26653" class="Bound">T</a><a id="26654" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26656" href="NbE.html#26656" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26658" href="NbE.html#26658" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26660" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="26664" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="26668" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="26670" href="NbE.html#26670" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="26672" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26674" href="NbE.html#26674" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="26677" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="26679" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26681" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="26684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26685" href="NbE.html#26656" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26687" href="NbE.html#26731" class="Function">a</a><a id="26688" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26691" href="NbE.html#26658" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26693" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26695" href="NbE.html#26649" class="Bound">S</a><a id="26696" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26698" class="Keyword">in</a>
  <a id="26703" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="26705" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="26707" href="NbE.html#26670" class="Bound">𝓋</a> <a id="26709" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="26711" href="NbE.html#20715" class="InductiveConstructor">nf-abs</a> <a id="26718" href="NbE.html#26674" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="26721" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
  <a id="26725" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="26731" href="NbE.html#26731" class="Function">a</a> <a id="26733" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26735" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="26738" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26739" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="26742" href="NbE.html#26649" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="26744" href="NbE.html#26658" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26745" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
With these two functions in place, we can define the reflection of a context
Γ into an environment. This will be the reflected environment over which a typed
term in the context Γ will be evaluated.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="↑ᶜᵗˣ"></a><a id="26959" href="NbE.html#26959" class="Function">↑ᶜᵗˣ</a> <a id="26964" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26966" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26968" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26969" href="NbE.html#26969" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26971" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26973" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="26976" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26978" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26980" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="26982" href="NbE.html#26969" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26984" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a>
<a id="26986" href="NbE.html#26959" class="Function">↑ᶜᵗˣ</a> <a id="26991" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a>       <a id="26999" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27001" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
<a id="27004" href="NbE.html#26959" class="Function">↑ᶜᵗˣ</a> <a id="27009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27010" href="NbE.html#27010" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27012" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27014" href="NbE.html#27014" class="Bound">T</a><a id="27015" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27017" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27019" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="27021" href="NbE.html#26959" class="Function">↑ᶜᵗˣ</a> <a id="27026" href="NbE.html#27010" class="Bound">Γ</a>  <a id="27029" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27031" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="27034" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27035" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="27038" href="NbE.html#27014" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27040" href="NbE.html#27010" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="27041" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27043" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>
We also need to use reflection and reification to
define the interpretation of primitive recursion in
System T, which must work with liftable neutrals (as
our interpretation of nat now has them embedded)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="rec↑"></a><a id="27262" href="NbE.html#27262" class="Function">rec↑</a> <a id="27267" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27269" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27271" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27272" href="NbE.html#27272" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27274" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27276" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="27280" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27282" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27284" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="27288" href="NbE.html#27272" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27290" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27292" href="NbE.html#22785" class="Function">Nf↑</a> <a id="27296" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27297" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="27301" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="27303" href="NbE.html#27272" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27305" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="27307" href="NbE.html#27272" class="Bound">T</a><a id="27308" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27310" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27312" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="27316" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="27320" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27322" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="27326" href="NbE.html#27272" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="27328" href="NbE.html#27262" class="Function">rec↑</a> <a id="27333" href="NbE.html#27333" class="Bound">𝓋̂z</a> <a id="27337" href="NbE.html#27337" class="Bound">𝓋̂s</a> <a id="27341" href="NbE.html#27341" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="27344" href="NbE.html#27344" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27346" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="27351" href="NbE.html#27341" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="27354" href="NbE.html#27344" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="27356" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="27360" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27362" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#809" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="27367" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a> <a id="27370" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27372" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#809" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="27377" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
<a id="27380" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="27384" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27386" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="27391" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="27393" href="NbE.html#27393" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="27395" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27397" href="NbE.html#27397" class="Bound">pf-𝓊</a> <a id="27402" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="27404" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="27408" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="27412" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="27414" href="NbE.html#27414" class="Bound">𝓋z</a> <a id="27417" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27419" href="NbE.html#27419" class="Bound">pf-𝓋z</a> <a id="27425" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="27427" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27429" class="Bound">𝓋̂z</a> <a id="27433" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27435" class="Keyword">in</a>
  <a id="27440" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="27444" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="27446" href="NbE.html#27446" class="Bound">𝓋s</a> <a id="27449" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27451" href="NbE.html#27451" class="Bound">pf-𝓋s</a> <a id="27457" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="27459" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27461" class="Bound">𝓋̂s</a> <a id="27465" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27467" class="Keyword">in</a>
  <a id="27472" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="27477" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="27479" href="NbE.html#4199" class="InductiveConstructor">rec</a> <a id="27483" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="27485" href="NbE.html#27414" class="Bound">𝓋z</a> <a id="27488" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="27490" href="NbE.html#27446" class="Bound">𝓋s</a> <a id="27493" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="27495" href="NbE.html#27393" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="27497" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27499" href="NbE.html#20115" class="InductiveConstructor">ne-rec</a> <a id="27506" href="NbE.html#27419" class="Bound">pf-𝓋z</a> <a id="27512" href="NbE.html#27451" class="Bound">pf-𝓋s</a> <a id="27518" href="NbE.html#27397" class="Bound">pf-𝓊</a> <a id="27523" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>

<a id="⟦rec⟧"></a><a id="27526" href="NbE.html#27526" class="Function">⟦rec⟧</a> <a id="27532" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27534" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27536" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27537" href="NbE.html#27537" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27539" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27541" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="27545" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27547" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27549" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="27551" href="NbE.html#27537" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27553" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="27555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27556" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="27560" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="27562" href="NbE.html#27537" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27564" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="27566" href="NbE.html#27537" class="Bound">T</a><a id="27567" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27569" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="27571" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="27575" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="27577" href="NbE.html#27537" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27579" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a>
<a id="27581" href="NbE.html#27526" class="Function">⟦rec⟧</a> <a id="27587" href="NbE.html#27587" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="27589" href="NbE.html#27589" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="27591" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>       <a id="27602" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27604" href="NbE.html#27587" class="Bound">z</a>
<a id="27606" href="NbE.html#27526" class="Function">⟦rec⟧</a> <a id="27612" href="NbE.html#27612" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="27614" href="NbE.html#27614" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="27616" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27617" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="27621" href="NbE.html#27621" class="Bound">n</a><a id="27622" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="27627" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27629" href="NbE.html#27614" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="27631" href="NbE.html#27621" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="27633" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27634" href="NbE.html#27526" class="Function">⟦rec⟧</a> <a id="27640" href="NbE.html#27612" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="27642" href="NbE.html#27614" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="27644" href="NbE.html#27621" class="Bound">n</a><a id="27645" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27647" href="NbE.html#27526" class="Function">⟦rec⟧</a> <a id="27653" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27654" href="NbE.html#27654" class="Bound">T</a><a id="27655" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27657" href="NbE.html#27657" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="27659" href="NbE.html#27659" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="27661" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27662" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="27665" href="NbE.html#27665" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="27667" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27669" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="27673" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="27676" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27677" href="NbE.html#27262" class="Function">rec↑</a> <a id="27682" href="NbE.html#27700" class="Function">𝓋̂z</a> <a id="27686" href="NbE.html#27713" class="Function">𝓋̂s</a> <a id="27690" href="NbE.html#27665" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="27692" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27694" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="27700" href="NbE.html#27700" class="Function">𝓋̂z</a> <a id="27704" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27706" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="27709" href="NbE.html#27657" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="27711" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="27713" href="NbE.html#27713" class="Function">𝓋̂s</a> <a id="27717" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27719" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="27722" href="NbE.html#27659" class="Bound">s</a>
</pre>
Now that we have a concrete interpretation of types,
and an interpretation for primitive recursion,
we can define the corresponding interpretations of
the lookup and typing judgements.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="⟦_∋Γ⟧"></a><a id="27922" href="NbE.html#27922" class="Function Operator">⟦_∋Γ⟧</a> <a id="27928" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27930" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="27932" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27933" href="NbE.html#27933" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27935" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27937" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="27940" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27942" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27943" href="NbE.html#27943" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27945" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27947" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="27951" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27953" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27955" href="NbE.html#27933" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27957" href="NbE.html#3455" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="27959" href="NbE.html#27943" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27961" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27963" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="27965" href="NbE.html#27933" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27967" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="27969" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27971" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="27973" href="NbE.html#27943" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="27975" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a>
<a id="27977" href="NbE.html#27922" class="Function Operator">⟦_∋Γ⟧</a> <a id="27983" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="27984" href="NbE.html#27984" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="27986" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27988" href="NbE.html#27988" class="Bound">T</a><a id="27989" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="27991" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="27994" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="27996" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="27998" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28000" href="NbE.html#28000" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="28002" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>     <a id="28008" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28010" href="NbE.html#28000" class="Bound">a</a>

</pre>
Finally, the algorithm for normalization by evaluation is as follows
<pre class="Agda"><a id="nbe"></a><a id="28343" href="NbE.html#28343" class="Function">nbe</a> <a id="28347" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28349" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="28351" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28352" href="NbE.html#28352" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28354" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28356" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="28359" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28361" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28362" href="NbE.html#28362" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="28364" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28366" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="28370" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28372" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28374" href="NbE.html#28352" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28376" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="28378" href="NbE.html#28362" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="28380" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28382" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="28385" href="NbE.html#28385" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="28387" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">]</a> <a id="28389" href="NbE.html#19591" class="Datatype">Nf</a> <a id="28392" href="NbE.html#28362" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="28394" href="NbE.html#28352" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28396" href="NbE.html#28385" class="Bound">t</a>
<a id="28398" href="NbE.html#28343" class="Function">nbe</a> <a id="28402" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28403" href="NbE.html#28403" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="28404" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28406" href="NbE.html#28406" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="28408" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28410" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="28413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28414" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟦⊢</a> <a id="28417" href="NbE.html#28406" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="28419" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟧</a> <a id="28421" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28422" href="NbE.html#26959" class="Function">↑ᶜᵗˣ</a> <a id="28427" href="NbE.html#28403" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="28428" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="28431" href="NbE.html#28403" class="Bound">Γ</a>

<a id="nf"></a><a id="28434" href="NbE.html#28434" class="Function">nf</a> <a id="28437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28439" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="28441" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28442" href="NbE.html#28442" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28444" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28446" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="28449" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28451" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28452" href="NbE.html#28452" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="28454" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28456" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="28460" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28462" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28464" href="NbE.html#28442" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28466" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="28468" href="NbE.html#28452" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="28470" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28472" href="NbE.html#28442" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="28474" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="28476" href="NbE.html#28452" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="28478" href="NbE.html#28434" class="Function">nf</a> <a id="28481" href="NbE.html#28481" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="28483" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28485" class="Keyword">let</a> <a id="28489" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="28491" href="NbE.html#28491" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="28494" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="28496" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="28498" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="28500" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28502" href="NbE.html#28343" class="Function">nbe</a> <a id="28506" href="NbE.html#28481" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="28508" class="Keyword">in</a> <a id="28511" href="NbE.html#28491" class="Bound">t′</a>
</pre>
And here we have some examples of the algorithm in action, reusing our
examples from [SystemT](./SystemT.lagda.md)

<pre class="Agda"><a id="28643" class="Comment">-- normal form of (λx. x) zero is zero</a>
<a id="nf-ex1"></a><a id="28682" href="NbE.html#28682" class="Function">nf-ex1</a> <a id="28689" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28691" href="NbE.html#28434" class="Function">nf</a> <a id="28694" href="NbE.html#4747" class="Function">ex1</a> <a id="28698" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#151" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="28700" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>
