<a id="nf-ex3"></a><a id="28951" href="NbE.html#28951" class="Function">nf-ex3</a> <a id="28958" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28960" href="NbE.html#28434" class="Function">nf</a> <a id="28963" href="NbE.html#4846" class="Function">ex3</a> <a id="28967" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#151" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="28969" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28970" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="28974" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="28976" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28977" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="28981" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="28983" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="28985" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28986" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a><a id="28988" class="Symbol">)))</a>
<a id="28992" href="NbE.html#28951" class="Function">nf-ex3</a> <a id="28999" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="29004" href="NbE.html#4846" class="Function">ex3</a>
<a id="29008" href="NbE.html#28951" class="Function">...</a>       <a id="29018" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="29020" class="Symbol">_</a>   <a id="29024" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29026" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#208" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>
As for the soundness properties we want from this algorithm:
  - `Γ ⊢ nf(t) : T` (well-typedness)
      We are using an intrinsically typed
      representation of terms, so this property is
      given to us automatically

  - `⟦ nf(t) ⟧ = ⟦ t ⟧` (preservation of meaning)
      We will prove this in the following section
      using definitional equality

  - `nf(nf(t)) = nf(t)` (idempotency)
      This follows directly from the preservation of
      meaning and completeness properties of the algorithm:

      By the soundness property of preservation of meaning,
      we have `Γ ⊢ nf t = t : T`, which implies `nf (nf t) = nf(t)`
      by completeness

For proving the completeness property of NbE,
our goal is to prove that two programs with the
same meaning (i.e. definitionally equal) have the
same normal form:

    Γ ⊢ t = t′ : T implies nf(t) = nf(t′)

We can prove this using some equational reasoning
paired with the definitional equality of two
terms impliying they are semantically equal
(included as a postulate for now)

<pre class="Agda"><a id="30086" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
  <a id="==→⟦≡⟧"></a><a id="30098" href="NbE.html#30098" class="Postulate">==→⟦≡⟧</a> <a id="30105" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30107" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="30109" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30110" href="NbE.html#30110" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="30112" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30114" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="30117" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30119" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30120" href="NbE.html#30120" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="30122" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30124" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="30128" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30130" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30131" href="NbE.html#30131" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="30133" href="NbE.html#30133" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="30136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30138" href="NbE.html#30110" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="30140" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="30142" href="NbE.html#30120" class="Bound">T</a><a id="30143" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30145" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="30146" href="NbE.html#30146" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="30148" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30150" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="30152" href="NbE.html#30110" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="30154" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="30155" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="30166" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30168" href="NbE.html#30131" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="30170" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="30173" href="NbE.html#30133" class="Bound">t′</a>
         <a id="30185" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30187" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟦⊢</a> <a id="30190" href="NbE.html#30131" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="30192" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟧</a> <a id="30194" href="NbE.html#30146" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="30196" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#151" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="30198" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟦⊢</a> <a id="30201" href="NbE.html#30133" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="30204" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟧</a> <a id="30206" href="NbE.html#30146" class="Bound">ρ</a>

<a id="31665" class="Comment">-- Proof of context extension is irrelevant, and any</a>
<a id="31718" class="Comment">-- two proofs that a context is an extension of another</a>
<a id="31774" class="Comment">-- are equivalent</a>

<a id="32769" class="Comment">-- Applying a shifted renaming to a variable is equivalent</a>
<a id="32828" class="Comment">-- to incrementing the original renaming of the variable&#39;s</a>
<a id="32887" class="Comment">-- lookup judgemnet:</a>

          <a id="33056" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33058" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="33060" href="NbE.html#33020" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33062" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="33064" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="33074" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33075" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">_↑ᵣ</a> <a id="33079" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="33080" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="33082" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33084" href="NbE.html#33007" class="Bound">S</a><a id="33085" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="33087" href="NbE.html#33032" class="Bound">σᵣ</a><a id="33089" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33091" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="33093" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#151" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="33095" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="33097" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33098" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="33101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33102" href="NbE.html#7440" class="Function">rename</a> <a id="33109" href="NbE.html#33020" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="33111" href="NbE.html#33032" class="Bound">σᵣ</a><a id="33113" class="Symbol">))</a>
