# Soundness

We prove the soundness property of preservation of meaning of NbE
(i.e. `⟦ nf(t) ⟧ = ⟦ t ⟧`), which we just call soundness here for brevity,
by proving the definitional equality of a term and its normal form:

    Γ ⊢ t = nf(t) : T

which expands to:

    Γ ⊢ t = ↓ᵀ a Γ, where a = ⟦ t ⟧ ↑Γ

For this, a logical relation `t Ⓡ a` is defined such that
it implies `Γ ⊢ t = ↓ᵀ a Γ : T`.

For defining the relation in Agda, we will need some functions first. The first
"lifts" definitional equality over liftable neutrals. Formally, this represents the condition `Γ ⊢ 𝓊 = 𝓊̂(Γ) : T`, or equivalently in Agda:
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_==↑_"></a><a id="37730" href="NbE.html#37730" class="Function Operator">_==↑_</a> <a id="37736" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37738" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="37739" href="NbE.html#37739" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="37741" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37743" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="37746" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="37748" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="37749" href="NbE.html#37749" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="37751" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37753" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="37757" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="37759" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37761" href="NbE.html#37739" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="37763" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="37765" href="NbE.html#37749" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="37767" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37769" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="37773" href="NbE.html#37749" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="37775" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37777" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
<a id="37781" href="NbE.html#37730" class="Function Operator">_==↑_</a> <a id="37787" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="37788" href="NbE.html#37788" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="37789" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="37791" href="NbE.html#37791" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="37793" href="NbE.html#37793" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="37796" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="37801" href="NbE.html#37793" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="37804" href="NbE.html#37788" class="Bound">Γ</a>
<a id="37806" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="37810" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="37812" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="37817" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="37819" href="NbE.html#37819" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="37821" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="37823" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="37825" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="37827" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="37835" class="Comment">-- If the liftable neutral can be lifted to the</a>
      <a id="37889" class="Comment">-- context Γ, this is just definitional equality</a>
      <a id="37944" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="37946" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="37949" href="NbE.html#37819" class="Bound">𝓊</a>
<a id="37951" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="37955" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="37957" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#809" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="37962" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="37964" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="37972" class="Comment">-- Otherwise, the proposition cannot be proven,</a>
      <a id="38026" class="Comment">-- as there is no lifted term in the context</a>
      <a id="38077" class="Comment">-- to compare a term to</a>
      <a id="38107" href="Data.Empty.html#526" class="Datatype">⊥</a>

<a id="38110" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="38116" class="Number">3</a> <a id="38118" href="NbE.html#37730" class="Function Operator">_==↑_</a>
</pre>
We also provide shorthand for reifying the interpretation of a term t
and then immediately applying a context Γ (we use lowercase γ as our
subscript as Γ is not a valid subscript)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="↓ᵀᵧ"></a><a id="38317" href="NbE.html#38317" class="Function">↓ᵀᵧ</a> <a id="38321" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38323" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="38325" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38326" href="NbE.html#38326" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="38328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38330" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="38333" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38335" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38336" href="NbE.html#38336" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="38338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38340" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="38344" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38346" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38348" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38349" href="NbE.html#38349" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="38351" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38353" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="38355" href="NbE.html#38336" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="38357" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="38358" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38360" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38362" href="NbE.html#38326" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="38364" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="38366" href="NbE.html#38336" class="Bound">T</a>
<a id="38368" href="NbE.html#38317" class="Function">↓ᵀᵧ</a> <a id="38372" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38373" href="NbE.html#38373" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="38374" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38376" href="NbE.html#38376" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="38378" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="38383" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="38386" href="NbE.html#38376" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="38388" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="38392" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="38394" href="NbE.html#38394" class="Bound">a↑</a> <a id="38397" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="38399" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="38405" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38406" href="NbE.html#38394" class="Bound">a↑</a> <a id="38409" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="38410" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
With these, we can begin to introduce the Kripe logical relation `Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ a`
between a typed term `Γ ⊢ t : T` and a value `a ∈ ⟦ T ⟧`. The logical relation
will be defined inductively on types. At type nat, the relation is defined as:

    Γ : nat Ⓡ 𝓋̂ ⇔ ∀ Γ′ ≤ Γ. Γ′ ⊢ t = 𝓋̂(Γ′) : nat

For Agda's termination checking, we have to define the logical relation at type
nat separately, which we do so in the form of Ⓝ:
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_Ⓝ_"></a><a id="38846" href="NbE.html#38846" class="Function Operator">_Ⓝ_</a> <a id="38850" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38852" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="38854" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38855" href="NbE.html#38855" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="38857" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38859" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="38862" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38864" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38866" href="NbE.html#38855" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="38868" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="38870" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="38874" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38876" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="38878" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="38882" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="38884" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="38886" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
</pre>
We define Ⓝ mutually with ==ℕ̂, a relation representing
the condition `Γ′ ⊢ t = 𝓋̂(Γ′) : nat`, which lifts definitional equality to
be over naturals with embedded liftable neutrals

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_==ℕ̂_"></a><a id="39085" href="NbE.html#39085" class="Function Operator">_==ℕ̂_</a> <a id="39092" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39094" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="39096" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="39097" href="NbE.html#39097" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="39099" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39101" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="39104" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="39106" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39108" href="NbE.html#39097" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="39110" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="39112" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="39116" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39118" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="39120" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="39124" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="39126" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39128" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>

<a id="39133" href="NbE.html#38846" class="Function Operator">_Ⓝ_</a> <a id="39137" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="39138" href="NbE.html#39138" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="39139" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="39141" href="NbE.html#39141" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="39143" href="NbE.html#39143" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a> <a id="39146" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="39150" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="39152" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="39153" href="NbE.html#39153" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="39156" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39158" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="39161" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="39165" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39167" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39168" href="NbE.html#39168" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="39173" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="39175" href="NbE.html#39153" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="39178" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="39180" href="NbE.html#39138" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="39181" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="39187" class="Comment">---------------</a>
  <a id="39205" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="39207" href="NbE.html#39168" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="39212" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="39215" href="NbE.html#39141" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="39217" href="NbE.html#39085" class="Function Operator">==ℕ̂</a> <a id="39222" href="NbE.html#39143" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a>

<a id="39226" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="39232" class="Number">4</a> <a id="39234" href="NbE.html#38846" class="Function Operator">_Ⓝ_</a>
</pre>
For `zero`, the ==ℕ̂ relation is a simple definitional equality
judgement:
<pre class="Agda"><a id="39326" href="NbE.html#39085" class="Function Operator">_==ℕ̂_</a> <a id="39333" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="39334" href="NbE.html#39334" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="39335" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="39337" href="NbE.html#39337" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="39339" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="39344" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39346" href="NbE.html#39337" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="39348" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="39351" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>
</pre>However, for our recursive case (suc 𝓋̂), the definition is a bit
more involved. We want the term to be definitionally equal to `suc · n`
such that n is logically related to 𝓋̂, a condition stronger than ==ℕ̂,
as it holds for all extensions of the context -- this is why we need
to define ==ℕ̂ mutually with Ⓝ. We want our recursive condition to be
stronger to have an easier time with the embedded liftable neutrals
<pre class="Agda"><a id="39785" href="NbE.html#39085" class="Function Operator">_==ℕ̂_</a> <a id="39792" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="39793" href="NbE.html#39793" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="39794" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="39796" href="NbE.html#39796" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="39798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39799" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="39803" href="NbE.html#39803" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a><a id="39805" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39807" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39809" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="39812" href="NbE.html#39812" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="39814" href="Data.Product.html#1806" class="Function">]</a> <a id="39816" href="NbE.html#39796" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="39818" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="39821" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="39825" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="39827" href="NbE.html#39812" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="39829" href="Data.Product.html#1167" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="39831" href="NbE.html#39812" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="39833" href="NbE.html#38846" class="Function Operator">Ⓝ</a> <a id="39835" href="NbE.html#39803" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a>
</pre>For an embedded liftable neutral, the relation is the
lifted definitional equality defined earlier
<pre class="Agda"><a id="39949" href="NbE.html#39085" class="Function Operator">_==ℕ̂_</a> <a id="39956" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="39957" href="NbE.html#39957" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="39958" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="39960" href="NbE.html#39960" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="39962" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39963" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="39966" href="NbE.html#39966" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="39968" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39970" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="39972" href="NbE.html#39960" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="39974" href="NbE.html#37730" class="Function Operator">==↑</a> <a id="39978" href="NbE.html#39966" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a>

<a id="39982" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="39988" class="Number">3</a> <a id="39990" href="NbE.html#39085" class="Function Operator">_==ℕ̂_</a>
</pre>
With these in place, we can start defining the logical
relation Ⓡ itself by induction on types, using Ⓝ for
the base type nat
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_Ⓡ_"></a><a id="40136" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">_Ⓡ_</a> <a id="40140" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40142" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="40144" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40145" href="NbE.html#40145" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="40147" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40149" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="40152" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40154" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40155" href="NbE.html#40155" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="40157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40159" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="40163" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40165" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40167" href="NbE.html#40145" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="40169" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="40171" href="NbE.html#40155" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="40173" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40175" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="40177" href="NbE.html#40155" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="40179" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a> <a id="40181" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40183" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>

<a id="40188" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">_Ⓡ_</a> <a id="40192" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40193" href="NbE.html#40193" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="40194" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40196" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40197" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="40200" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40202" href="NbE.html#40202" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="40204" href="NbE.html#40204" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a> <a id="40207" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40209" href="NbE.html#40202" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="40211" href="NbE.html#38846" class="Function Operator">Ⓝ</a> <a id="40213" href="NbE.html#40204" class="Bound">𝓋̂</a>
</pre>
For function types, the relation is defined as:
    Γ ⊢ r : S → T Ⓡ f ⇔ ∀ Γ′ ≤ Γ. Γ′ ⊢ s : S Ⓡ a ⇒ Γ′ ⊢ r s : T Ⓡ f(a)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="40348" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">_Ⓡ_</a> <a id="40352" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40353" href="NbE.html#40353" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="40354" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40356" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40357" href="NbE.html#40357" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="40359" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="40361" href="NbE.html#40361" class="Bound">T</a><a id="40362" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40364" href="NbE.html#40364" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="40366" href="NbE.html#40366" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="40368" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="40372" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="40374" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40375" href="NbE.html#40375" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="40378" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40380" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="40383" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="40387" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40390" href="NbE.html#40390" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="40395" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40397" href="NbE.html#40375" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="40400" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="40402" href="NbE.html#40353" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="40403" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="40407" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40409" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="40411" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40412" href="NbE.html#40412" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="40414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40416" href="NbE.html#40375" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="40419" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="40421" href="NbE.html#40357" class="Bound">S</a><a id="40422" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40424" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40425" href="NbE.html#40425" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="40427" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40429" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="40431" href="NbE.html#40357" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="40433" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="40434" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="40438" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40440" href="NbE.html#40412" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="40442" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="40444" href="NbE.html#40425" class="Bound">a</a>
    <a id="40450" class="Comment">----------------------</a>
  <a id="40475" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40477" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40478" href="NbE.html#40390" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="40483" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="40486" href="NbE.html#40364" class="Bound">r</a><a id="40487" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="40489" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="40491" href="NbE.html#40412" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="40493" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="40495" href="NbE.html#40366" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="40497" href="NbE.html#40425" class="Bound">a</a>

<a id="40500" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="40506" class="Number">4</a> <a id="40508" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">_Ⓡ_</a>
</pre>
A result of defining our Kripe logical relation in terms
of definitional equality is that the relation is transitive
with respect to definitional equality
<pre class="Agda"><a id="==-Ⓡ-trans"></a><a id="40680" href="NbE.html#40680" class="Function">==-Ⓡ-trans</a> <a id="40691" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40693" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="40695" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40696" href="NbE.html#40696" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="40698" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40700" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="40703" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40705" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40706" href="NbE.html#40706" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="40708" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40710" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="40714" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40716" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40717" href="NbE.html#40717" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="40719" href="NbE.html#40719" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="40722" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40724" href="NbE.html#40696" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="40726" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="40728" href="NbE.html#40706" class="Bound">T</a><a id="40729" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40731" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40732" href="NbE.html#40732" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="40734" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="40736" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="40738" href="NbE.html#40706" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="40740" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="40741" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="40754" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40756" href="NbE.html#40717" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="40758" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="40761" href="NbE.html#40719" class="Bound">t′</a>
           <a id="40775" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40777" href="NbE.html#40717" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="40779" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="40781" href="NbE.html#40732" class="Bound">a</a>
             <a id="40796" class="Comment">-------</a>
           <a id="40815" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="40817" href="NbE.html#40719" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="40820" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="40822" href="NbE.html#40732" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="40824" href="NbE.html#40680" class="Function">==-Ⓡ-trans</a> <a id="40835" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40836" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="40838" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40840" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="40843" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40845" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40846" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="40848" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40850" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="40854" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40856" href="NbE.html#40856" class="Bound">t==t′</a> <a id="40862" href="NbE.html#40862" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="40865" href="NbE.html#40865" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="40870" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="40874" href="NbE.html#14451" class="InductiveConstructor">trans</a> <a id="40880" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40881" href="NbE.html#14350" class="InductiveConstructor">sym</a> <a id="40885" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40886" href="NbE.html#36156" class="Postulate">==-subst</a> <a id="40895" href="NbE.html#40856" class="Bound">t==t′</a><a id="40900" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="40903" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="40904" href="NbE.html#40862" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="40907" href="NbE.html#40865" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="40911" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="40913" href="NbE.html#40680" class="Function">==-Ⓡ-trans</a> <a id="40924" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40925" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="40927" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40929" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="40932" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40934" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="40935" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="40937" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="40939" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="40943" href="NbE.html#40943" class="Bound">a</a><a id="40944" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="40946" href="NbE.html#40946" class="Bound">t==t′</a> <a id="40952" href="NbE.html#40952" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="40955" href="NbE.html#40955" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
  <a id="40962" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="40967" href="NbE.html#40952" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="40970" href="NbE.html#40955" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
<a id="40975" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="40979" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="40981" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="40983" href="NbE.html#40983" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="40985" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="40987" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="40989" href="NbE.html#40989" class="Bound">t==sn</a> <a id="40995" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="40997" href="NbE.html#40997" class="Bound">n==a</a> <a id="41002" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="41004" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="41006" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="41010" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="41012" href="NbE.html#40983" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="41014" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41016" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="41018" href="NbE.html#14451" class="InductiveConstructor">trans</a> <a id="41024" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41025" href="NbE.html#14350" class="InductiveConstructor">sym</a> <a id="41029" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41030" href="NbE.html#36156" class="Postulate">==-subst</a> <a id="41039" class="Bound">t==t′</a><a id="41044" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="41047" href="NbE.html#40989" class="Bound">t==sn</a> <a id="41053" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41055" href="NbE.html#40997" class="Bound">n==a</a> <a id="41060" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="41062" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="41064" href="NbE.html#40680" class="Function">==-Ⓡ-trans</a> <a id="41075" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41076" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="41078" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41080" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="41083" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41085" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41086" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="41088" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41090" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="41093" href="NbE.html#41093" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="41095" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41097" href="NbE.html#41097" class="Bound">t==t′</a> <a id="41103" href="NbE.html#41103" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41106" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41107" href="NbE.html#41107" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="41109" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41111" href="NbE.html#41111" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
  <a id="41118" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="41123" href="NbE.html#41093" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="41126" href="NbE.html#41107" class="Bound">Γ′</a>          <a id="41138" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="41140" href="NbE.html#41103" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41143" href="NbE.html#41111" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
<a id="41148" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="41152" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="41154" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="41159" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="41161" href="NbE.html#41161" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="41163" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="41165" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="41167" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="41169" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="41171" href="NbE.html#41171" class="Bound">t==𝓊</a> <a id="41176" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="41180" href="NbE.html#14451" class="InductiveConstructor">trans</a> <a id="41186" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41187" href="NbE.html#14350" class="InductiveConstructor">sym</a> <a id="41191" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41192" href="NbE.html#36156" class="Postulate">==-subst</a> <a id="41201" class="Bound">t==t′</a><a id="41206" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="41209" href="NbE.html#41171" class="Bound">t==𝓊</a>
<a id="41214" href="NbE.html#40680" class="Function">==-Ⓡ-trans</a> <a id="41225" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41226" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="41228" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41230" href="NbE.html#41230" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="41232" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="41234" href="NbE.html#41234" class="Bound">T</a><a id="41235" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41237" href="NbE.html#41237" class="Bound">t==t′</a> <a id="41243" href="NbE.html#41243" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41246" href="NbE.html#41246" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="41251" href="NbE.html#41251" class="Bound">sⓇa</a> <a id="41255" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="41259" href="NbE.html#40680" class="Function">==-Ⓡ-trans</a> <a id="41270" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41271" href="NbE.html#14012" class="InductiveConstructor">app-compatible</a> <a id="41286" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41287" href="NbE.html#36156" class="Postulate">==-subst</a> <a id="41296" href="NbE.html#41237" class="Bound">t==t′</a><a id="41301" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41303" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="41307" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41309" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41310" href="NbE.html#41243" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41313" href="NbE.html#41246" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="41318" href="NbE.html#41251" class="Bound">sⓇa</a><a id="41321" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Additionally, because we have defined the relation so that its implication
holds for all extensions of a context, we can "weaken" the logical relation
`Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ a` for all `Γ′ ≤ Γ`, having that `Γ′ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ a` holds as well
<pre class="Agda"><a id="Ⓡ-weaken"></a><a id="41564" href="NbE.html#41564" class="Function">Ⓡ-weaken</a> <a id="41573" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41575" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="41577" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41578" href="NbE.html#41578" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="41581" href="NbE.html#41581" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="41583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41585" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="41588" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41590" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41591" href="NbE.html#41591" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="41593" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41595" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="41599" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41601" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41602" href="NbE.html#41602" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="41607" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41609" href="NbE.html#41578" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="41612" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="41614" href="NbE.html#41581" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="41615" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41618" href="NbE.html#41618" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="41620" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41622" href="NbE.html#41581" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="41624" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="41626" href="NbE.html#41591" class="Bound">T</a><a id="41627" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41629" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41630" href="NbE.html#41630" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="41632" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41634" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="41636" href="NbE.html#41591" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="41638" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="41639" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="41647" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41649" href="NbE.html#41618" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="41651" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="41653" href="NbE.html#41630" class="Bound">a</a>
      <a id="41661" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41663" href="NbE.html#41602" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="41668" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="41671" href="NbE.html#41618" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="41673" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="41675" href="NbE.html#41630" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="41677" href="NbE.html#41564" class="Function">Ⓡ-weaken</a> <a id="41686" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41687" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="41689" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41691" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="41694" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41696" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41697" href="NbE.html#41697" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="41701" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41703" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41704" href="NbE.html#41704" class="Bound">t</a><a id="41705" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41707" href="NbE.html#41707" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41710" href="NbE.html#41710" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a>
  <a id="41718" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="41726" href="NbE.html#35802" class="Postulate">weaken-compose</a> <a id="41741" href="NbE.html#41710" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="41747" href="NbE.html#41697" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="41752" href="NbE.html#41704" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="41754" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41756" href="NbE.html#41707" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41759" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41760" href="NbE.html#32150" class="Function">≤-trans</a> <a id="41768" href="NbE.html#41710" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="41774" href="NbE.html#41697" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="41778" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="41780" href="NbE.html#41564" class="Function">Ⓡ-weaken</a> <a id="41789" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41790" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="41792" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41794" href="NbE.html#41794" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="41796" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="41798" href="NbE.html#41798" class="Bound">T</a><a id="41799" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41801" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41802" href="NbE.html#41802" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="41806" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41808" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="41809" href="NbE.html#41809" class="Bound">t</a><a id="41810" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="41812" href="NbE.html#41812" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41815" href="NbE.html#41815" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="41821" href="NbE.html#41821" class="Bound">sⓇa</a>
  <a id="41827" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="41835" href="NbE.html#35802" class="Postulate">weaken-compose</a> <a id="41850" href="NbE.html#41815" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="41856" href="NbE.html#41802" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="41861" href="NbE.html#41809" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="41863" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="41865" href="NbE.html#41812" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="41868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41869" href="NbE.html#32150" class="Function">≤-trans</a> <a id="41877" href="NbE.html#41815" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="41883" href="NbE.html#41802" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="41887" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41889" href="NbE.html#41821" class="Bound">sⓇa</a>
</pre>
The Kripke logical relation is "sandwiched" between
reflection and reification -- to arrive at the logical
relation between a term and a semantic object, the
semantic object must be a reflection of a liftable neutral
that is definitionally equal to the term. Likewise,
if a logical relation holds between a term and a semantic
object, then the term must be definitionally equal
to the reification of that semantic object.

This is intentional, as these results will be exactly
what we will need to prove the soundness of NbE. We
formalize them with the following implications, which
we will prove mutually (as reflection and reification
are themselves defined mutually) by induction on types.

Our first implication is:

    (∀ Γ′ ≤ Γ. Γ′ ⊢ 𝓊 = 𝓊̂(Γ) : T) ⇒ Γ ⊢ 𝓊 : T Ⓡ ↑ᵀ 𝓊̂

which we can now formalize in Agda with our definitions
<pre class="Agda"><a id="==↑-Ⓡ"></a><a id="42739" href="NbE.html#42739" class="Function">==↑-Ⓡ</a> <a id="42745" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42747" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="42749" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="42750" href="NbE.html#42750" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="42752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42754" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="42757" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="42759" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="42760" href="NbE.html#42760" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="42762" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42764" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="42768" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="42770" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="42771" href="NbE.html#42771" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="42773" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42775" href="NbE.html#42750" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="42777" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="42779" href="NbE.html#42760" class="Bound">T</a><a id="42780" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="42782" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="42783" href="NbE.html#42783" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="42786" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42788" href="NbE.html#22701" class="Function">Ne↑</a> <a id="42792" href="NbE.html#42760" class="Bound">T</a><a id="42793" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="42801" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42803" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="42806" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="42807" href="NbE.html#42807" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="42810" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42812" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="42815" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="42826" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42828" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="42829" href="NbE.html#42829" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="42834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="42836" href="NbE.html#42807" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="42839" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="42841" href="NbE.html#42750" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="42842" class="Symbol">)</a>
         <a id="42853" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42855" href="NbE.html#42829" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="42860" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="42863" href="NbE.html#42771" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="42865" href="NbE.html#37730" class="Function Operator">==↑</a> <a id="42869" href="NbE.html#42783" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="42871" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="42881" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
      <a id="42907" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="42909" href="NbE.html#42771" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="42911" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="42913" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="42914" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="42917" href="NbE.html#42783" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="42919" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
The second implication is:

    Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ a ⇒ ∀ Γ′ ≤ Γ. Γ′ ⊢ t = ↓ᵀ a Γ′ : T

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Ⓡ-==↓"></a><a id="43014" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="43020" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43022" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="43024" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43025" href="NbE.html#43025" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="43028" href="NbE.html#43028" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="43030" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43032" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="43035" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43037" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43038" href="NbE.html#43038" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="43040" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43042" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="43046" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43048" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43049" href="NbE.html#43049" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="43051" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43053" href="NbE.html#43028" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="43055" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="43057" href="NbE.html#43038" class="Bound">T</a><a id="43058" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43060" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43061" href="NbE.html#43061" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="43063" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43065" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="43067" href="NbE.html#43038" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="43069" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="43070" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="43078" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43080" href="NbE.html#43049" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="43082" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="43084" href="NbE.html#43061" class="Bound">a</a>
        <a id="43094" class="Comment">---------------------</a>
      <a id="43122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43124" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="43125" href="NbE.html#43125" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="43130" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43132" href="NbE.html#43025" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="43135" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="43137" href="NbE.html#43028" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="43138" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="43146" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43148" href="NbE.html#43125" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="43153" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="43156" href="NbE.html#43049" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="43158" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="43161" href="NbE.html#38317" class="Function">↓ᵀᵧ</a> <a id="43165" href="NbE.html#43061" class="Bound">a</a>
</pre>
A consequence of the first implication is that
`Γ , x:T ⊢ x Ⓡ ↑ᵀ (𝓍̂ Γ)`, which we define now
as it will be the lemma we will need for proving the
second implication
<pre class="Agda"><a id="xⓇ↑ᵀ𝓍̂"></a><a id="43346" href="NbE.html#43346" class="Function">xⓇ↑ᵀ𝓍̂</a> <a id="43353" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43355" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="43357" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43358" href="NbE.html#43358" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="43360" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43362" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="43365" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43367" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43368" href="NbE.html#43368" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="43370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="43372" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="43376" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="43386" class="Comment">-------------------------</a>
      <a id="43418" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="43420" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="43422" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="43425" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43426" href="NbE.html#43358" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="43427" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43429" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43430" href="NbE.html#43368" class="Bound">T</a><a id="43431" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43433" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="43435" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="43438" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="43439" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="43442" href="NbE.html#43368" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="43444" href="NbE.html#43358" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="43445" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
To prove the first implication, first we show that it always
holds for liftable neutral terms of type nat. This is simply
the given proof, so this case follows immediately.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="43633" href="NbE.html#42739" class="Function">==↑-Ⓡ</a> <a id="43639" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="43640" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="43642" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="43644" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="43647" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="43649" href="NbE.html#43649" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="43652" href="NbE.html#43652" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="43657" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="43659" href="NbE.html#43649" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="43662" href="NbE.html#43652" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
</pre>Now, for liftable neutral terms of type S → T, we prove that
the relation holds for `↑ᵀ (𝓊̂ · ↓ˢ a)`

We prove the relation holds by using our induction
hypothesis, so that our new goal is to prove that

    Γ″ ⊢ 𝓊 s = (𝓊̂ · (↓ˢ a)) Γ″ : T

for any Γ″ that is an extension of Γ′ (which itself
extends Γ).

Note that `(𝓊̂ · (↓ˢ a)) Γ″` is equivalent to
`𝓊̂(Γ″) · (↓ˢ a)(Γ″)` (application of liftable neutrals is overloaded.

First, we deconstruct `𝓊̂ (Γ″)`,
using our given proof that it's definitionally
equal to `Γ″ ⊢ 𝓊 : S → T` to both discard the case
where `𝓊̂ (Γ″)` is undefined and simplify our goal
to proving that:

    Γ″ ⊢ 𝓊 · s = 𝓊″ · ↓ˢ a Γ″ : T (𝓊″ is 𝓊̂ lifted to the context Γ″)

We also use the other implication we will prove,
alongside the fact that `s Ⓡ a`, to have evidence
that `Γ″ ⊢ s : S` is definitionally equal to
`↓ˢ a Γ″`.

With these pieces in place, we can use equational reasoning for definitional
equality to prove the desired goal.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="44643" href="NbE.html#42739" class="Function">==↑-Ⓡ</a> <a id="44649" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44650" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="44652" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="44654" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="44656" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="44658" class="Symbol">_}</a> <a id="44661" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44662" href="NbE.html#44662" class="Bound">𝓊</a><a id="44663" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44665" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44666" href="NbE.html#44666" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="44668" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44670" href="NbE.html#44670" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="44673" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44674" href="NbE.html#44674" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="44676" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44678" href="NbE.html#44678" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="44683" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44684" href="NbE.html#44684" class="Bound">s</a><a id="44685" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44687" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44688" href="NbE.html#44688" class="Bound">a</a><a id="44689" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44691" href="NbE.html#44691" class="Bound">sⓇa</a> <a id="44695" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="44699" href="NbE.html#42739" class="Function">==↑-Ⓡ</a> <a id="44705" href="NbE.html#44733" class="Function">𝓊·s==𝓊̂·↓ˢa</a>
    <a id="44721" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="44733" href="NbE.html#44733" class="Function">𝓊·s==𝓊̂·↓ˢa</a> <a id="44745" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44747" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="44749" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44750" href="NbE.html#44750" class="Bound">Γ″</a> <a id="44753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44755" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="44758" class="Symbol">}</a>
                 <a id="44777" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44779" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44780" href="NbE.html#44780" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="44786" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44788" href="NbE.html#44750" class="Bound">Γ″</a> <a id="44791" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="44793" href="NbE.html#44674" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="44795" class="Symbol">)</a>
                 <a id="44814" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="44816" href="NbE.html#44780" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="44822" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="44825" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44826" href="NbE.html#44678" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="44831" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="44834" href="NbE.html#44662" class="Bound">𝓊</a><a id="44835" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44837" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="44839" href="NbE.html#44684" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="44841" href="NbE.html#37730" class="Function Operator">==↑</a> <a id="44845" href="NbE.html#44666" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="44848" href="NbE.html#22927" class="Function Operator">·↑</a> <a id="44851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44852" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="44855" href="NbE.html#44688" class="Bound">a</a><a id="44856" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="44864" href="NbE.html#44733" class="Function">𝓊·s==𝓊̂·↓ˢa</a>  <a id="44877" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="44878" href="NbE.html#44878" class="Bound">Γ″</a><a id="44880" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="44882" href="NbE.html#44882" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a>
        <a id="44896" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="44901" href="NbE.html#44666" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="44904" href="NbE.html#44878" class="Bound">Γ″</a>           <a id="44917" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="44919" href="NbE.html#44670" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="44922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44923" href="NbE.html#32150" class="Function">≤-trans</a> <a id="44931" href="NbE.html#44882" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="44937" href="NbE.html#44678" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="44941" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="44949" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="44953" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="44955" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="44960" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="44962" href="NbE.html#44962" class="Bound">𝓊″</a> <a id="44965" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="44967" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="44969" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="44971" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="44973" href="NbE.html#44973" class="Bound">𝓊==𝓊″</a>
        <a id="44987" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="44992" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="44998" href="NbE.html#44691" class="Bound">sⓇa</a> <a id="45002" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a>
      <a id="45014" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="45018" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="45020" href="NbE.html#45020" class="Bound">s==↓ᵀᵧa</a> <a id="45028" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="45038" href="NbE.html#14842" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
          <a id="45054" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="45060" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="45063" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45064" href="NbE.html#44678" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="45069" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="45072" href="NbE.html#44662" class="Bound">𝓊</a><a id="45073" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="45075" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="45077" href="NbE.html#44684" class="Bound">s</a>
        <a id="45087" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="45091" href="NbE.html#14012" class="InductiveConstructor">app-compatible</a> <a id="45106" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45107" href="NbE.html#30441" class="Function">≡→==</a> <a id="45112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45113" href="NbE.html#35802" class="Postulate">weaken-compose</a> <a id="45128" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="45134" href="NbE.html#44678" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="45139" href="NbE.html#44662" class="Bound">𝓊</a><a id="45140" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="45143" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="45148" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
          <a id="45160" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45161" href="NbE.html#45352" class="Function">Γ″≤Γ</a> <a id="45166" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="45169" href="NbE.html#44662" class="Bound">𝓊</a><a id="45170" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="45172" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="45174" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45175" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="45181" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="45184" href="NbE.html#44684" class="Bound">s</a><a id="45185" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="45195" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="45199" href="NbE.html#14012" class="InductiveConstructor">app-compatible</a> <a id="45214" class="Bound">𝓊==𝓊″</a> <a id="45220" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="45225" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
          <a id="45237" class="Bound">𝓊″</a> <a id="45240" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="45242" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="45243" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="45249" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="45252" href="NbE.html#44684" class="Bound">s</a><a id="45253" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="45263" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="45267" href="NbE.html#14012" class="InductiveConstructor">app-compatible</a> <a id="45282" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="45287" href="NbE.html#45020" class="Bound">s==↓ᵀᵧa</a> <a id="45295" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
          <a id="45307" class="Bound">𝓊″</a> <a id="45310" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="45312" href="NbE.html#38317" class="Function">↓ᵀᵧ</a> <a id="45316" href="NbE.html#44688" class="Bound">a</a>
        <a id="45326" href="NbE.html#15125" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
        <a id="45336" class="Keyword">where</a>
          <a id="45352" href="NbE.html#45352" class="Function">Γ″≤Γ</a> <a id="45357" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="45359" href="NbE.html#32150" class="Function">≤-trans</a> <a id="45367" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="45373" href="NbE.html#44678" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
</pre>
To prove the second implication, we proceed similarly
and first prove it for type nat. If the term is logically
related to zero, the implication holds immediately from
our given proof
<pre class="Agda"><a id="45575" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="45581" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="45582" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="45584" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="45586" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="45589" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="45591" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="45592" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="45594" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="45596" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="45600" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="45602" href="NbE.html#45602" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="45605" href="NbE.html#45605" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="45610" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="45615" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="45618" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="45619" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="45622" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="45624" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>
<a id="45629" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="45633" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="45635" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="45637" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="45639" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="45642" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
</pre>Otherwise, if the term is logically related to
a successor of a natural, our given proof
similarly leads to the implication, though for this case,
we additionally need a lemma showing
that if a term of type nat is definitionally
equal to an object a of type ℕ̂ (i.e. a natural
with embedded liftable neutrals), then it is
definitionally equal to the reification of
the object a. We can prove this by induction
on a.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="46075" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="46081" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46082" href="NbE.html#46082" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="46083" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46085" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46086" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="46088" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46090" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="46093" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46095" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46096" href="NbE.html#46096" class="Bound">t</a><a id="46097" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46099" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46100" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="46104" href="NbE.html#46104" class="Bound">a</a><a id="46105" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46107" href="NbE.html#46107" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="46110" href="NbE.html#46110" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
  <a id="46117" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="46122" href="NbE.html#46107" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="46125" href="NbE.html#46110" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
<a id="46130" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="46134" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46136" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="46138" href="NbE.html#46138" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="46140" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="46142" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="46144" href="NbE.html#46144" class="Bound">t==sn</a> <a id="46150" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="46152" href="NbE.html#46152" class="Bound">nⓇa</a> <a id="46156" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="46158" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
  <a id="46162" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="46167" href="NbE.html#46152" class="Bound">nⓇa</a> <a id="46171" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a>
<a id="46176" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="46180" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46182" href="NbE.html#46182" class="Bound">n==ℕ̂a</a> <a id="46189" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="46197" href="NbE.html#34681" class="Function">[id]-identity</a> <a id="46211" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46212" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="46214" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46216" class="Bound">n</a><a id="46217" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46219" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="46223" href="NbE.html#14842" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
    <a id="46233" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="46238" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="46241" class="Bound">t</a>
  <a id="46245" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="46249" class="Bound">t==sn</a> <a id="46255" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="46261" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="46265" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="46267" class="Bound">n</a>
  <a id="46271" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="46275" href="NbE.html#14012" class="InductiveConstructor">app-compatible</a> <a id="46290" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="46295" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="46296" href="NbE.html#46356" class="Function">==ℕ̂→==↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46306" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46307" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="46309" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46311" class="Bound">a</a><a id="46312" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46314" href="NbE.html#46182" class="Bound">n==ℕ̂a</a><a id="46320" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="46322" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="46328" href="NbE.html#4176" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="46332" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="46334" href="NbE.html#38317" class="Function">↓ᵀᵧ</a> <a id="46338" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="46342" href="NbE.html#15125" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
  <a id="46346" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="46356" href="NbE.html#46356" class="Function">==ℕ̂→==↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46366" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="46368" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="46370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46371" href="NbE.html#46371" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="46373" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="46375" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="46378" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46380" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46381" href="NbE.html#46381" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="46383" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="46385" href="NbE.html#46371" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="46387" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="46389" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="46392" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46394" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46395" href="NbE.html#46395" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="46397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="46399" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="46401" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a> <a id="46405" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="46406" class="Symbol">}</a>
             <a id="46421" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="46423" href="NbE.html#46381" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="46425" href="NbE.html#39085" class="Function Operator">==ℕ̂</a> <a id="46430" href="NbE.html#46395" class="Bound">a</a>
               <a id="46447" class="Comment">----------</a>
             <a id="46471" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="46473" href="NbE.html#46381" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="46475" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="46478" href="NbE.html#38317" class="Function">↓ᵀᵧ</a> <a id="46482" href="NbE.html#46395" class="Bound">a</a>
    <a id="46488" href="NbE.html#46356" class="Function">==ℕ̂→==↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46498" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46499" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="46501" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46503" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="46507" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46509" href="NbE.html#46509" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="46512" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="46517" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46520" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46521" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="46524" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46526" href="NbE.html#23599" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>
    <a id="46535" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="46539" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46541" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="46543" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46545" class="Bound">pf</a>
    <a id="46552" href="NbE.html#46356" class="Function">==ℕ̂→==↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46562" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46563" href="NbE.html#46563" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="46564" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46566" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46567" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="46569" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46571" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="46575" href="NbE.html#46575" class="Bound">a</a><a id="46576" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46578" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="46580" href="NbE.html#46580" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="46582" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="46584" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="46586" href="NbE.html#46586" class="Bound">m==sn</a> <a id="46592" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="46594" href="NbE.html#46594" class="Bound">n==a</a> <a id="46599" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="46601" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
      <a id="46609" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="46614" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46618" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="46621" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46623" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="46624" href="NbE.html#23611" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="46628" href="NbE.html#46575" class="Bound">a</a><a id="46629" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="46631" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46633" href="NbE.html#46356" class="Function">==ℕ̂→==↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46643" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46644" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="46646" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46648" href="NbE.html#46575" class="Bound">a</a><a id="46649" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46651" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="46652" href="NbE.html#46594" class="Bound">n==a</a> <a id="46657" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a><a id="46661" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="46667" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="46671" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46673" class="Symbol">_</a>                 <a id="46691" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46693" href="NbE.html#46693" class="Bound">pf</a>
      <a id="46702" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="46710" href="NbE.html#34681" class="Function">[id]-identity</a> <a id="46724" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46725" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="46727" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46729" class="Bound">n</a><a id="46730" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46732" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46734" href="NbE.html#14451" class="InductiveConstructor">trans</a> <a id="46740" class="Bound">m==sn</a> <a id="46746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="46747" href="NbE.html#14012" class="InductiveConstructor">app-compatible</a> <a id="46762" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="46767" href="NbE.html#46693" class="Bound">pf</a><a id="46769" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="46775" href="NbE.html#46356" class="Function">==ℕ̂→==↓ᵀ</a> <a id="46785" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46786" href="NbE.html#46786" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="46787" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46789" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46790" href="NbE.html#46790" class="Bound">t</a><a id="46791" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46793" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="46794" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="46797" href="NbE.html#46797" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="46799" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="46801" href="NbE.html#46801" class="Bound">pf</a>
      <a id="46810" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="46815" href="NbE.html#46797" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="46818" href="NbE.html#46786" class="Bound">Γ</a>           <a id="46830" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46832" href="NbE.html#46801" class="Bound">pf</a>
    <a id="46839" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="46843" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46845" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="46850" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="46852" href="NbE.html#46852" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="46854" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="46856" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="46858" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="46860" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="46862" href="NbE.html#46862" class="Bound">t==𝓊</a> <a id="46867" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="46869" href="NbE.html#46862" class="Bound">t==𝓊</a>
</pre>Lastly for type nat, if the term is logically related to an
embedded liftable neutral, the implication also
holds immediately from our given proof
<pre class="Agda"><a id="47033" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="47039" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="47040" href="NbE.html#47040" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="47042" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="47044" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="47045" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="47047" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="47049" href="NbE.html#851" class="InductiveConstructor">nat</a><a id="47052" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="47054" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="47055" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="47057" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="47059" href="NbE.html#23627" class="InductiveConstructor">ne</a> <a id="47062" href="NbE.html#47062" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a><a id="47064" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="47066" href="NbE.html#47066" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="47069" href="NbE.html#47069" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
  <a id="47076" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="47081" href="NbE.html#47062" class="Bound">𝓊̂</a> <a id="47084" href="NbE.html#47040" class="Bound">Γ′</a>           <a id="47097" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="47099" href="NbE.html#47066" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="47102" href="NbE.html#47069" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a>
<a id="47107" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="47111" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="47113" href="Data.Sum.Base.html#784" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="47118" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="47120" href="NbE.html#47120" class="Bound">𝓊</a> <a id="47122" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="47124" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="47126" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>  <a id="47129" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="47131" href="NbE.html#47131" class="Bound">t==𝓊</a>     <a id="47140" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="47142" href="NbE.html#47131" class="Bound">t==𝓊</a>
</pre>For our inductive step, we prove the implication
for terms of type S → T. Our desired implication
is now:

    Γ′ ⊢ t = ↓ᵀ f Γ′ : T

which, by definition, expands to:

    Γ′ ⊢ t = λx. ↓ᵀ f a (Γ′ , x:S) : T (where a = ↑ᵀ 𝓍̂ˢ Γ′)

We prove this by η expanding t to `λx. t x` and
then using the compatibility rule for abstractions
of definitional equality to simplify our goal to
proving:

    Γ′ , x:S ⊢ t x = ↓ᵀ f a (Γ′, x:S)

Note that our inductive hypothesis is:

    t x Ⓡ f a implies t x = ↓ᵀ f a

This is exactly what we want to show, so now
all we need is to prove that `t x Ⓡ f a`.

Luckily, our given proof holds that t and f
are logically related, which is equivalent
to saying that if `x Ⓡ a` , then `t x Ⓡ f a`,
reducing what we have to prove only to
`x Ⓡ a`. We have been using "a" for simplicity,
but `a = ↑ᵀ 𝓍̂ˢ Γ′`, and we are mutually proving
that `x Ⓡ ↑ᵀ 𝓍̂`, so we use this lemma here
to finish our proof.
<pre class="Agda"><a id="48084" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="48090" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48091" href="NbE.html#48091" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="48093" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48095" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48096" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="48098" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="48100" href="NbE.html#48100" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="48102" href="NbE.html#864" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="48104" class="Symbol">_}</a> <a id="48107" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48108" href="NbE.html#48108" class="Bound">t</a><a id="48109" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48111" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48112" href="NbE.html#48112" class="Bound">f</a><a id="48113" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48115" href="NbE.html#48115" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="48118" href="NbE.html#48118" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="48123" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="48127" href="NbE.html#14842" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
    <a id="48137" href="NbE.html#48118" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="48142" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="48145" href="NbE.html#48108" class="Bound">t</a>
  <a id="48149" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="48153" href="NbE.html#13514" class="InductiveConstructor">η</a> <a id="48155" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="48161" href="NbE.html#4368" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="48163" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48164" href="NbE.html#48100" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="48166" href="NbE.html#11820" class="Function Operator">↑⊢</a> <a id="48169" href="NbE.html#48118" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="48174" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="48177" href="NbE.html#48108" class="Bound">t</a><a id="48178" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="48180" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="48182" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="48184" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a>
  <a id="48189" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a>
    <a id="48197" href="NbE.html#13853" class="InductiveConstructor">abs-compatible</a> <a id="48212" class="Symbol">(</a>
      <a id="48220" href="NbE.html#14842" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
        <a id="48234" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48235" href="NbE.html#48100" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="48237" href="NbE.html#11820" class="Function Operator">↑⊢</a> <a id="48240" href="NbE.html#48118" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="48245" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="48248" href="NbE.html#48108" class="Bound">t</a><a id="48249" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="48251" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="48253" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="48255" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a>
      <a id="48264" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="48268" href="NbE.html#14012" class="InductiveConstructor">app-compatible</a> <a id="48283" href="NbE.html#48476" class="Function">subst-lemma</a> <a id="48295" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="48300" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
        <a id="48310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48311" href="NbE.html#2724" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-ext</a> <a id="48317" href="NbE.html#48118" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="48322" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="48325" href="NbE.html#48108" class="Bound">t</a><a id="48326" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="48328" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="48330" href="NbE.html#11520" class="Function">subst-id</a> <a id="48339" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="48341" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="48343" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="48345" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a>
      <a id="48354" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="48358" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="48364" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48365" href="NbE.html#48115" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="48368" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48369" href="NbE.html#2724" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-ext</a> <a id="48375" href="NbE.html#48118" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="48379" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="48381" href="NbE.html#48595" class="Function">xⓇa</a><a id="48384" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="48386" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a> <a id="48391" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
        <a id="48401" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="48407" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48408" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="48411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48412" href="NbE.html#48112" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="48414" href="NbE.html#48570" class="Function">a</a><a id="48415" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="48417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48418" href="NbE.html#48091" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="48421" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="48423" href="NbE.html#48100" class="Bound">S</a><a id="48424" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="48433" href="NbE.html#15125" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
  <a id="48437" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="48438" href="NbE.html#14952" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="48444" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="48450" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48451" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="48454" href="NbE.html#48112" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="48456" href="NbE.html#48091" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="48458" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="48462" href="NbE.html#15125" class="Function Operator">∎</a>
  <a id="48466" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="48476" href="NbE.html#48476" class="Function">subst-lemma</a> <a id="48488" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="48496" href="NbE.html#30441" class="Function">≡→==</a> <a id="48501" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48502" href="NbE.html#547" class="Function">≡-trans</a> <a id="48510" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48511" href="NbE.html#36448" class="Function">incr-↑-≡</a> <a id="48520" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48521" class="Argument">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="48526" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="48528" href="NbE.html#48118" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="48532" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48534" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48535" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="48537" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="48539" href="NbE.html#48108" class="Bound">t</a><a id="48540" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="48543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48544" href="NbE.html#531" class="Function">≡-sym</a> <a id="48550" href="NbE.html#34681" class="Function">[id]-identity</a><a id="48563" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="48570" href="NbE.html#48570" class="Function">a</a> <a id="48572" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="48574" href="NbE.html#24056" class="Function">↑ᵀ</a> <a id="48577" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48578" href="NbE.html#48100" class="Bound">S</a><a id="48579" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48581" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48582" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="48585" href="NbE.html#48100" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="48587" href="NbE.html#48091" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="48589" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="48595" href="NbE.html#48595" class="Function">xⓇa</a> <a id="48599" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="48601" href="NbE.html#43346" class="Function">xⓇ↑ᵀ𝓍̂</a> <a id="48608" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48609" href="NbE.html#48091" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="48611" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48613" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48614" href="NbE.html#48100" class="Bound">S</a><a id="48615" class="Symbol">}</a>
</pre>
Using our first implication, we can quickly
prove that `Γ , x:T ⊢ x : T Ⓡ ↑ᵀ 𝓍̂`, as `Γ′ ⊢ x = 𝓍̂ Γ′ : T` for all
`Γ′ ≤ Γ , x:T`
<pre class="Agda"><a id="48759" href="NbE.html#43346" class="Function">xⓇ↑ᵀ𝓍̂</a> <a id="48766" class="Symbol">{_}</a> <a id="48770" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48771" href="NbE.html#48771" class="Bound">T</a><a id="48772" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48774" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="48776" href="NbE.html#42739" class="Function">==↑-Ⓡ</a> <a id="48782" href="NbE.html#48796" class="Function">x==𝓍̂</a> <a id="48788" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="48796" href="NbE.html#48796" class="Function">x==𝓍̂</a> <a id="48802" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="48804" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="48806" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48807" href="NbE.html#48807" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="48809" href="NbE.html#48809" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="48812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="48814" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="48817" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="48826" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="48828" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48829" href="NbE.html#48829" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ,T</a> <a id="48836" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="48838" href="NbE.html#48809" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="48841" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="48843" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48844" href="NbE.html#48807" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="48846" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="48848" href="NbE.html#48771" class="Bound">T</a><a id="48849" class="Symbol">))</a>
       <a id="48859" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="48861" href="NbE.html#48829" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ,T</a> <a id="48868" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="48871" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="48873" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="48876" href="NbE.html#37730" class="Function Operator">==↑</a> <a id="48880" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="48883" href="NbE.html#48771" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="48885" href="NbE.html#48807" class="Bound">Γ</a>
  <a id="48889" href="NbE.html#48796" class="Function">x==𝓍̂</a> <a id="48895" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48896" href="NbE.html#48896" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="48897" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48899" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="48900" href="NbE.html#48900" class="Bound">Γ′</a><a id="48902" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="48904" href="NbE.html#48904" class="Bound">pf</a>
    <a id="48911" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="48916" href="NbE.html#48900" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="48919" href="NbE.html#2934" class="Function Operator">≤?</a> <a id="48922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="48923" href="NbE.html#48896" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="48925" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="48927" href="NbE.html#48771" class="Bound">T</a><a id="48928" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="48932" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="48936" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="48938" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1685" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="48941" href="NbE.html#48941" class="Bound">¬pf</a> <a id="48945" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="48947" href="NbE.html#48941" class="Bound">¬pf</a> <a id="48951" class="Bound">pf</a>
  <a id="48956" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="48960" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="48962" href="Relation.Nullary.html#1648" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="48966" href="NbE.html#48966" class="Bound">pf′</a>
    <a id="48974" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="48979" href="NbE.html#26017" class="Function">𝓍̂</a> <a id="48982" href="NbE.html#48771" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="48984" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="48986" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="48988" href="NbE.html#31792" class="Function">≤-pf-irrelevance</a> <a id="49005" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="49008" href="NbE.html#48966" class="Bound">pf′</a>
  <a id="49014" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="49018" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="49020" class="Symbol">_</a>      <a id="49027" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="49029" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#208" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
    <a id="49038" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="49043" href="NbE.html#9364" class="Function">ren-≤</a> <a id="49049" class="Bound">pf′</a>
  <a id="49055" class="Symbol">...|</a> <a id="49060" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="49062" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="49064" class="Symbol">_</a>  <a id="49067" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="49069" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>
Before moving forward, we also want to show that rec Ⓡ ⟦rec⟧.
This will be necessary for proving soundness, as we will need
proof that `Γ ⊢ rec = ↓ᵀ ⟦rec⟧ Γ : (T ⇒ (nat ⇒ T ⇒ T) ⇒ nat ⇒ T)`
(i.e. proof that our interpretation of rec is sound) to prove the
soundness of NbE
