        <a id="52175" href="NbE.html#52175" class="Function">subst-lemma₄</a> <a id="52188" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="52190" href="NbE.html#531" class="Function">≡-sym</a> <a id="52196" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="52197" href="NbE.html#35802" class="Postulate">weaken-compose</a> <a id="52212" class="Bound">Γ⁗≤Γ‴</a> <a id="52218" href="NbE.html#51156" class="Function">Γ‴≤Γ′</a> <a id="52224" href="NbE.html#50531" class="Bound">z</a><a id="52225" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="52235" href="NbE.html#52235" class="Function">subst-lemma₅</a>  <a id="52249" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="52251" href="NbE.html#531" class="Function">≡-sym</a> <a id="52257" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="52258" href="NbE.html#35802" class="Postulate">weaken-compose</a> <a id="52273" href="NbE.html#50566" class="Bound">Γ‴≤Γ″</a> <a id="52279" href="NbE.html#50542" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="52285" href="NbE.html#50531" class="Bound">z</a><a id="52286" class="Symbol">)</a>

        <a id="52297" href="NbE.html#52297" class="Function">z==↓ᵀaz</a> <a id="52305" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="52307" class="Bound">Γ⁗≤Γ‴</a> <a id="52313" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="52316" href="NbE.html#50566" class="Bound">Γ‴≤Γ″</a> <a id="52322" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="52325" href="NbE.html#50542" class="Bound">Γ″≤Γ′</a> <a id="52331" href="NbE.html#11261" class="Function Operator">≤⊢</a> <a id="52334" href="NbE.html#50531" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="52336" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="52339" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="52345" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="52346" href="NbE.html#24162" class="Function">↓ᵀ</a> <a id="52349" href="NbE.html#50535" class="Bound">az</a> <a id="52352" class="Bound">Γ⁗</a><a id="52354" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="52364" href="NbE.html#52297" class="Function">z==↓ᵀaz</a>
          <a id="52382" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="52387" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="52393" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="52394" class="Bound">Γ⁗</a><a id="52396" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="52398" href="NbE.html#50539" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="52401" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="52402" href="NbE.html#32150" class="Function">≤-trans</a> <a id="52410" class="Bound">Γ⁗≤Γ‴</a> <a id="52416" href="NbE.html#51156" class="Function">Γ‴≤Γ′</a><a id="52421" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="52431" href="NbE.html#52297" class="Function">...</a> <a id="52435" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="52437" href="NbE.html#52437" class="Bound">pf</a>
          <a id="52450" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="52458" href="NbE.html#52175" class="Function">subst-lemma₄</a> <a id="52471" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="52473" href="NbE.html#52235" class="Function">subst-lemma₅</a> <a id="52486" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="52488" href="NbE.html#52437" class="Bound">pf</a>
</pre>
With that out of the way, having proved the lemma that
`Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ a ⇒ ∀ Γ′ ≤ Γ. Γ′ ⊢ t = ↓ᵀ a Γ : T`, we have:
    Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ a ⇒ Γ ⊢ t = ↓ᵀ a Γ : T
which is what we wanted our logical relation to imply,
so that we can then show that `Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ a` for `a = ⟦t⟧ (↑ Γ)`

For this, we will establish that `Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ ⟦t⟧ (↑ Γ)`
using the fundamental lemma of logical relations. First,
we will need to extend logical relations to include
substitutions and environments. We again use ∥Ⓡ∥ for
the "parallel" in parallel substitutions, as Ⓡ is
already defined for terms and semantic objects
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_∥Ⓡ∥_"></a><a id="53094" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">_∥Ⓡ∥_</a> <a id="53100" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="53102" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="53104" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="53105" href="NbE.html#53105" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="53107" href="NbE.html#53107" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="53109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="53111" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="53114" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="53122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="53124" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="53128" href="NbE.html#53105" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="53130" href="NbE.html#53107" class="Bound">Δ</a>
      <a id="53138" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="53140" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="53142" href="NbE.html#53107" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="53144" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a>
      <a id="53152" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="53154" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
</pre>
Similarly as for terms and values, a Kripe logical
relation between a parallel substitution and an
environment is defined inductively, though this time
by induction on the rules for parallel substitutions
instead of by induction on types

A substitution from the empty context is always
logically related to an empty environment
<pre class="Agda"><a id="53500" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="53502" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="53506" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a> <a id="53509" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="53511" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#164" class="Record">⊤</a>
</pre>
An extension to a substition (σ , s / x) is logically
related to an environment (ρ , a) if σ is logically
related to ρ and s is logically related to a
<pre class="Agda"><a id="53677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="53678" href="NbE.html#53678" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="53680" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="53682" href="NbE.html#53682" class="Bound">s</a><a id="53683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="53685" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="53689" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="53691" href="NbE.html#53691" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="53693" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="53695" href="NbE.html#53695" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="53697" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="53699" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="53701" href="NbE.html#53678" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="53703" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="53707" href="NbE.html#53691" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="53709" href="Data.Product.html#1167" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="53711" href="NbE.html#53682" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="53713" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="53715" href="NbE.html#53695" class="Bound">a</a>

<a id="53718" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="53724" class="Number">4</a> <a id="53726" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">_∥Ⓡ∥_</a>
</pre>
A consequence of how substitutions and their logical
relation with environments are defined is that we
have that a logical relation for a shifted substitution
holds if the logical relation holds for the original
substitution (as the shifted terms will be irrelevant)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="∥Ⓡ∥-↑"></a><a id="54012" href="NbE.html#54012" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-↑</a> <a id="54018" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54020" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="54022" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54023" href="NbE.html#54023" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="54025" href="NbE.html#54025" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="54027" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54029" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="54032" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54034" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54035" href="NbE.html#54035" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="54037" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54039" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="54043" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54045" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54046" href="NbE.html#54046" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="54049" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54051" href="NbE.html#7046" class="Datatype">Ren</a> <a id="54055" href="NbE.html#54023" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="54057" href="NbE.html#54025" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="54058" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54060" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54061" href="NbE.html#54061" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="54063" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54065" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="54067" href="NbE.html#54025" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="54069" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="54070" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="54078" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="54080" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="54090" href="NbE.html#54046" class="Bound">σᵣ</a> <a id="54093" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="54097" href="NbE.html#54061" class="Bound">ρ</a>
      <a id="54105" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="54107" href="NbE.html#9605" class="Function">subst-ren</a> <a id="54117" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="54118" href="NbE.html#7979" class="Function Operator">_↑ᵣ</a> <a id="54122" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54123" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="54125" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54127" href="NbE.html#54035" class="Bound">T</a><a id="54128" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54130" href="NbE.html#54046" class="Bound">σᵣ</a><a id="54132" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="54134" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="54138" href="NbE.html#54061" class="Bound">ρ</a>
<a id="54140" href="NbE.html#54012" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-↑</a> <a id="54146" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54147" class="Argument">σᵣ</a> <a id="54150" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54152" href="NbE.html#7076" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a><a id="54153" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54155" href="NbE.html#54155" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="54158" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54160" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
<a id="54163" href="NbE.html#54012" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-↑</a> <a id="54169" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54170" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="54172" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54174" href="NbE.html#54174" class="Bound">T</a><a id="54175" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54177" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54178" class="Argument">σᵣ</a> <a id="54181" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54183" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="54185" href="NbE.html#7105" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="54187" href="NbE.html#54187" class="Bound">x</a><a id="54188" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54190" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54191" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="54193" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="54195" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="54197" href="NbE.html#54197" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="54199" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a><a id="54200" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54202" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="54204" href="NbE.html#54204" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="54207" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="54209" href="NbE.html#54209" class="Bound">xⓇa</a> <a id="54213" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="54215" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54217" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="54219" href="NbE.html#54012" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-↑</a> <a id="54225" href="NbE.html#54204" class="Bound">pf</a> <a id="54228" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="54230" href="NbE.html#54379" class="Function">↑⊢xⓇa</a> <a id="54236" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
  <a id="54240" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="54250" href="NbE.html#54250" class="Function">subst-lemma₁</a> <a id="54263" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54265" href="NbE.html#32980" class="Function">shift-var</a> <a id="54275" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54276" class="Argument">S</a> <a id="54278" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54280" href="NbE.html#54174" class="Bound">T</a><a id="54281" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54283" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54284" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="54286" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54288" href="NbE.html#54187" class="Bound">x</a><a id="54289" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54291" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54292" class="Argument">σᵣ</a> <a id="54295" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54297" href="NbE.html#9021" class="Function">ren-id</a><a id="54303" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="54309" href="NbE.html#54309" class="Function">subst-lemma₂</a> <a id="54322" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54324" href="NbE.html#33531" class="Function">rename-id</a> <a id="54334" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54335" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="54337" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54339" href="NbE.html#54187" class="Bound">x</a><a id="54340" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="54347" href="NbE.html#54347" class="Function">Γ,T≤Γ</a> <a id="54353" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54355" href="NbE.html#2724" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-ext</a> <a id="54361" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54362" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="54364" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54366" href="NbE.html#54174" class="Bound">T</a><a id="54367" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54369" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a>

    <a id="54379" href="NbE.html#54379" class="Function">↑⊢xⓇa</a> <a id="54385" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54387" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="54389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="54390" href="NbE.html#3553" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`S</a> <a id="54393" href="NbE.html#54187" class="Bound">x</a><a id="54394" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="54396" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="54398" href="NbE.html#54197" class="Bound">a</a>
    <a id="54404" href="NbE.html#54379" class="Function">↑⊢xⓇa</a>
      <a id="54416" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="54421" href="NbE.html#41564" class="Function">Ⓡ-weaken</a> <a id="54430" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54431" class="Argument">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="54436" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54438" href="NbE.html#54347" class="Function">Γ,T≤Γ</a><a id="54443" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54445" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54446" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="54448" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54450" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="54452" href="NbE.html#54187" class="Bound">x</a><a id="54453" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54455" href="NbE.html#54209" class="Bound">xⓇa</a>
    <a id="54463" href="NbE.html#54379" class="Function">...</a> <a id="54467" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="54469" href="NbE.html#54469" class="Bound">pf</a>
      <a id="54478" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="54486" href="NbE.html#54250" class="Function">subst-lemma₁</a> <a id="54499" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="54501" href="NbE.html#54309" class="Function">subst-lemma₂</a> <a id="54514" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54516" href="NbE.html#54469" class="Bound">pf</a>
</pre>
A generalization of this is, similarly as for logical relations
between terms and semantic objects, that if a logical relation
holds between a substitution and an environment, it holds for any
weakening of the substitution (as weakening is really a series
of shifts)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="∥Ⓡ∥-weaken"></a><a id="54799" href="NbE.html#54799" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-weaken</a> <a id="54810" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54812" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="54814" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54815" href="NbE.html#54815" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="54818" href="NbE.html#54818" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="54820" href="NbE.html#54820" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="54822" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54824" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="54827" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54829" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54830" href="NbE.html#54830" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="54835" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54837" href="NbE.html#54815" class="Bound">Γ′</a> <a id="54840" href="NbE.html#2664" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="54842" href="NbE.html#54818" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="54843" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54845" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54846" href="NbE.html#54846" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="54848" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54850" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="54854" href="NbE.html#54818" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="54856" href="NbE.html#54820" class="Bound">Δ</a><a id="54857" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54859" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54860" href="NbE.html#54860" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="54862" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="54864" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="54866" href="NbE.html#54820" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="54868" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="54869" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="54879" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="54881" href="NbE.html#54846" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="54883" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="54887" href="NbE.html#54860" class="Bound">ρ</a>
        <a id="54897" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="54899" href="NbE.html#54846" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="54901" href="NbE.html#10718" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="54903" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="54904" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="54911" href="NbE.html#54830" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="54915" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="54917" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="54921" href="NbE.html#54860" class="Bound">ρ</a>
<a id="54923" href="NbE.html#54799" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-weaken</a> <a id="54934" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54935" class="Argument">σ</a> <a id="54937" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54939" href="NbE.html#6499" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a><a id="54940" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54942" href="NbE.html#54942" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="54944" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54946" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
<a id="54949" href="NbE.html#54799" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-weaken</a> <a id="54960" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54961" class="Argument">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="54966" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="54968" href="NbE.html#54968" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="54972" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54974" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="54975" href="NbE.html#54975" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="54977" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="54979" href="NbE.html#54979" class="Bound">s</a><a id="54980" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="54982" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="54984" href="NbE.html#54984" class="Bound">σ∥Ⓡ∥ρ</a> <a id="54990" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="54992" href="NbE.html#54992" class="Bound">sⓇa</a> <a id="54996" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="54998" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="55002" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="55004" href="NbE.html#54799" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-weaken</a> <a id="55015" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55016" class="Argument">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="55021" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="55023" href="NbE.html#54968" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="55027" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55029" href="NbE.html#54984" class="Bound">σ∥Ⓡ∥ρ</a> <a id="55035" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="55037" href="NbE.html#41564" class="Function">Ⓡ-weaken</a> <a id="55046" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55047" class="Argument">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="55052" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="55054" href="NbE.html#54968" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="55058" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55060" href="NbE.html#54992" class="Bound">sⓇa</a> <a id="55064" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>
We are now ready to introduce the semantic typing judgement
`Γ ⊨ t : T`, which will be the what we will use to arrive
at `Γ ⊢ t : T Ⓡ ⟦ t ⟧ ↑Γ Γ`
<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊨_"></a><a id="55225" href="NbE.html#55225" class="Function Operator">_⊨_</a> <a id="55229" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55231" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="55233" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55234" href="NbE.html#55234" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="55236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55238" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="55242" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55244" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="55246" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="55247" href="NbE.html#55247" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="55249" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55251" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="55254" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="55256" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="55258" href="NbE.html#55247" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="55260" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="55262" href="NbE.html#55234" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="55264" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="55266" href="Agda.Primitive.html#326" class="Primitive">Set</a>
<a id="55270" href="NbE.html#55225" class="Function Operator">_⊨_</a> <a id="55274" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55275" href="NbE.html#55275" class="Bound">T</a><a id="55276" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55278" href="NbE.html#55278" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="55280" href="NbE.html#55280" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="55282" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="55286" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="55288" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55289" href="NbE.html#55289" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="55291" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55293" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="55296" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55298" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55299" href="NbE.html#55299" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="55301" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55303" href="NbE.html#6469" class="Datatype">Sub</a> <a id="55307" href="NbE.html#55289" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="55309" href="NbE.html#55278" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="55310" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55312" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55313" href="NbE.html#55313" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="55315" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55317" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟦</a> <a id="55319" href="NbE.html#55278" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="55321" href="NbE.html#15764" class="Field Operator">⟧</a><a id="55322" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="55326" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="55328" href="NbE.html#55299" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="55330" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="55334" href="NbE.html#55313" class="Bound">ρ</a>
    <a id="55340" class="Comment">-------</a>
  <a id="55350" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="55352" href="NbE.html#55280" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="55354" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="55356" href="NbE.html#55299" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="55358" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="55360" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="55362" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟦⊢</a> <a id="55365" href="NbE.html#55280" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="55367" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟧</a> <a id="55369" href="NbE.html#55313" class="Bound">ρ</a>
</pre>
By induction on the typing judgement `Γ ⊢ t : T`,
we prove the semantic typing judgement `Γ ⊨ t : T`,
this is called the fundamental lemma of logical
relations
<pre class="Agda"><a id="fundamental-lemma"></a><a id="55544" href="NbE.html#55544" class="Function">fundamental-lemma</a> <a id="55562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55564" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="55566" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55567" href="NbE.html#55567" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="55569" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55571" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="55574" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55576" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55577" href="NbE.html#55577" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="55579" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55581" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="55585" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55587" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55588" href="NbE.html#55588" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="55590" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="55592" href="NbE.html#55567" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="55594" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="55596" href="NbE.html#55577" class="Bound">T</a><a id="55597" class="Symbol">}</a>
                  <a id="55617" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="55619" href="NbE.html#55567" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="55621" href="NbE.html#55225" class="Function Operator">⊨</a> <a id="55623" href="NbE.html#55588" class="Bound">t</a>
<a id="55625" href="NbE.html#55544" class="Function">fundamental-lemma</a> <a id="55643" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="55644" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="55646" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="55648" href="NbE.html#4158" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="55652" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="55654" href="NbE.html#55654" class="Bound">σ∥Ⓡ∥ρ</a> <a id="55660" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="55662" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="55664" href="NbE.html#14269" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

      <a id="56328" href="NbE.html#35435" class="Postulate">subst-compose</a> <a id="56342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="56343" class="Argument">τ</a> <a id="56345" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="56347" href="NbE.html#11520" class="Function">subst-id</a> <a id="56356" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56358" href="NbE.html#56239" class="Bound">s</a><a id="56359" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="56361" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="56362" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="56369" href="NbE.html#56233" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="56374" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a> <a id="56376" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56378" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="56380" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a><a id="56382" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="56384" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="56385" href="NbE.html#56212" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="56387" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="56389" href="NbE.html#56220" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="56391" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a> <a id="56393" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56395" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="56397" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="56400" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="56401" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="56407" href="NbE.html#56407" class="Function">subst-lemma₂</a> <a id="56420" class="Symbol">=</a>

    <a id="56508" href="NbE.html#56508" class="Function">t[σ′]</a> <a id="56514" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="56516" href="NbE.html#56212" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="56518" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="56520" href="NbE.html#56220" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="56522" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a> <a id="56524" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56526" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="56528" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="56531" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="56533" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="56535" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="56542" href="NbE.html#56233" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="56547" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a> <a id="56549" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56551" href="NbE.html#4308" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="56553" href="NbE.html#3486" class="InductiveConstructor">`Z</a> <a id="56556" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a>

    <a id="56703" href="NbE.html#56703" class="Function">subst-lemma₅</a> <a id="56716" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="56718" href="NbE.html#35197" class="Function">id-compose-identity</a> <a id="56738" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="56739" class="Argument">σ</a> <a id="56741" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="56743" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="56750" href="NbE.html#56233" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="56754" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="56761" href="NbE.html#56761" class="Function">σ″</a> <a id="56764" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="56766" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="56768" href="NbE.html#56220" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="56770" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a><a id="56771" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="56773" href="NbE.html#10718" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="56775" class="Symbol">(((</a><a id="56778" href="NbE.html#11041" class="Function">weaken</a> <a id="56785" href="NbE.html#56233" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="56790" href="NbE.html#10033" class="Function Operator">↑</a><a id="56791" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="56793" href="NbE.html#10718" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="56795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="56796" href="NbE.html#11520" class="Function">subst-id</a> <a id="56805" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56807" href="NbE.html#56239" class="Bound">s</a><a id="56808" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="56811" href="NbE.html#6522" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56813" href="NbE.html#56239" class="Bound">s</a><a id="56814" class="Symbol">))</a>

    <a id="56822" href="NbE.html#56822" class="Function">σ″Ⓡρ</a> <a id="56827" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="56829" href="NbE.html#56761" class="Function">σ″</a>  <a id="56833" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="56837" href="NbE.html#56224" class="Bound">ρ</a>
    <a id="56843" href="NbE.html#56822" class="Function">σ″Ⓡρ</a> <a id="56848" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="56856" href="NbE.html#56563" class="Function">subst-lemma₃</a> <a id="56869" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="56871" href="NbE.html#56631" class="Function">subst-lemma₄</a> <a id="56884" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="56886" href="NbE.html#56703" class="Function">subst-lemma₅</a> <a id="56899" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="56907" href="NbE.html#54799" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-weaken</a> <a id="56918" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="56919" class="Argument">Γ′≤Γ</a> <a id="56924" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="56926" href="NbE.html#56233" class="Bound">Γ′≤Γ</a><a id="56930" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="56932" href="NbE.html#56227" class="Bound">σ∥Ⓡ∥ρ</a>

    <a id="56943" href="NbE.html#56943" class="Function">t[σ′][s/x]Ⓡ⟦t⟧⟨ρ,a⟩</a> <a id="56963" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="56965" href="NbE.html#56508" class="Function">t[σ′]</a> <a id="56971" href="NbE.html#12152" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="56973" href="NbE.html#56239" class="Bound">s</a> <a id="56975" href="NbE.html#12152" class="Function Operator">/x]</a> <a id="56979" href="NbE.html#40136" class="Function Operator">Ⓡ</a> <a id="56981" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟦⊢</a> <a id="56984" href="NbE.html#56212" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="56986" href="NbE.html#28056" class="Function Operator">⟧</a> <a id="56988" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="56990" href="NbE.html#56224" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="56992" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="56994" href="NbE.html#56243" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="56996" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="57002" href="NbE.html#56943" class="Function">t[σ′][s/x]Ⓡ⟦t⟧⟨ρ,a⟩</a> <a id="57022" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="57030" href="NbE.html#56307" class="Function">subst-lemma₁</a> <a id="57043" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="57045" href="NbE.html#56407" class="Function">subst-lemma₂</a> <a id="57058" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="57068" href="NbE.html#55544" class="Function">fundamental-lemma</a> <a id="57086" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57087" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="57089" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57091" href="NbE.html#56212" class="Bound">t</a><a id="57092" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="57094" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="57096" href="NbE.html#56822" class="Function">σ″Ⓡρ</a> <a id="57101" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="57103" href="NbE.html#56246" class="Bound">sⓇa</a> <a id="57107" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="57109" href="NbE.html#55544" class="Function">fundamental-lemma</a> <a id="57127" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57128" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="57130" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57132" href="NbE.html#57132" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="57134" href="NbE.html#4442" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="57136" href="NbE.html#57136" class="Bound">s</a><a id="57137" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="57139" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57140" class="Argument">σ</a> <a id="57142" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57144" href="NbE.html#57144" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="57145" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="57147" href="NbE.html#57147" class="Bound">σ∥Ⓡ∥ρ</a>
  <a id="57155" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="57160" href="NbE.html#55544" class="Function">fundamental-lemma</a> <a id="57178" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57179" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="57181" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57183" href="NbE.html#57132" class="Bound">r</a><a id="57184" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="57186" href="NbE.html#57147" class="Bound">σ∥Ⓡ∥ρ</a> <a id="57192" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="57194" href="NbE.html#55544" class="Function">fundamental-lemma</a> <a id="57212" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57213" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="57215" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57217" href="NbE.html#57136" class="Bound">s</a><a id="57218" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="57220" href="NbE.html#57147" class="Bound">σ∥Ⓡ∥ρ</a>
<a id="57226" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="57230" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="57232" href="NbE.html#57232" class="Bound">Γ⊨r</a>                              <a id="57265" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="57267" href="NbE.html#57267" class="Bound">Γ⊨s</a>
  <a id="57273" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="57278" href="NbE.html#57232" class="Bound">Γ⊨r</a> <a id="57282" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a> <a id="57287" href="NbE.html#57267" class="Bound">Γ⊨s</a>
<a id="57291" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="57295" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="57297" href="NbE.html#57297" class="Bound">pf</a>
  <a id="57302" class="Keyword">rewrite</a> <a id="57310" href="NbE.html#34681" class="Function">[id]-identity</a> <a id="57324" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57325" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="57327" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57329" class="Bound">r</a> <a id="57331" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="57333" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="57335" href="NbE.html#10309" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="57336" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="57338" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57340" href="NbE.html#57297" class="Bound">pf</a>
</pre>
For the identity substitution we have that `Γ ⊢ id : Γ Ⓡ ↑Γ` ,
which we prove by induction using our lemma that
`Γ,x:T ⊢ x : T Ⓡ ↑ᵀ (𝓍ᵀ Γ)` for every variable that we
are substituting for itself.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="idⓇ↑Γ"></a><a id="57553" href="NbE.html#57553" class="Function">idⓇ↑Γ</a> <a id="57559" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="57561" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="57563" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57564" href="NbE.html#57564" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="57566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="57568" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="57571" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="57580" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="57582" href="NbE.html#11520" class="Function">subst-id</a> <a id="57591" href="NbE.html#53094" class="Function Operator">∥Ⓡ∥</a> <a id="57595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="57596" href="NbE.html#26959" class="Function">↑ᶜᵗˣ</a> <a id="57601" href="NbE.html#57564" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="57602" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="57604" href="NbE.html#57553" class="Function">idⓇ↑Γ</a> <a id="57610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="57611" href="NbE.html#1742" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a><a id="57612" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="57614" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="57616" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#201" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>
</pre>For our inductive step, our IH will give us that
`Γ ⊢ id : Γ Ⓡ ↑Γ Γ`, but we want proof that `Γ , x:T ⊢ id ↑ : Γ Ⓡ Γ`
(because the identity substitution is unwrapped to `(id ↑ , x / x)`
for the context` Γ , x:T`). Here, we use our lemma that if a
logical relation holds for a substitution and an environment
it holds for a shifting of the substition, allowing us to
transform our IH into our goal
<pre class="Agda"><a id="58028" href="NbE.html#57553" class="Function">idⓇ↑Γ</a> <a id="58034" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58035" href="NbE.html#58035" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="58037" href="NbE.html#1752" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="58039" href="NbE.html#58039" class="Bound">T</a><a id="58040" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="58042" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="58044" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="58046" href="NbE.html#54012" class="Function">∥Ⓡ∥-↑</a> <a id="58052" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58053" class="Argument">T</a> <a id="58055" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="58057" href="NbE.html#58039" class="Bound">T</a><a id="58058" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="58060" href="NbE.html#57553" class="Function">idⓇ↑Γ</a> <a id="58066" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="58068" href="NbE.html#43346" class="Function">xⓇ↑ᵀ𝓍̂</a> <a id="58075" href="NbE.html#401" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>
With this fact, we arrive at the soundness of NbE. By the fundamental lemma,
given `Γ ⊢ id : Γ Ⓡ ↑Γ`, we have that `Γ ⊢ t [ id ] Ⓡ ⟦ t ⟧ ↑Γ` -- and
`t [ id ] ≡ t`.

Using the lemma that logical relation implies definitional
equality to the reified semantic object, we arrive at
`Γ ⊢ t = ↓ᵀᵧ ⟦ t ⟧ ↑Γ : T`, which is what we want to show
(i.e. `Γ ⊢ t = nf(t) : T`)
<pre class="Agda"><a id="soundness"></a><a id="58453" href="NbE.html#58453" class="Function">soundness</a> <a id="58463" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="58465" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="58467" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58468" href="NbE.html#58468" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="58470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="58472" href="NbE.html#1724" class="Datatype">Ctx</a><a id="58475" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="58477" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58478" href="NbE.html#58478" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="58480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="58482" href="NbE.html#832" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="58486" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="58488" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58489" href="NbE.html#58489" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="58491" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="58493" href="NbE.html#58468" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="58495" href="NbE.html#4123" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="58497" href="NbE.html#58478" class="Bound">T</a><a id="58498" class="Symbol">}</a>
          <a id="58510" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="58512" href="NbE.html#58489" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="58514" href="NbE.html#12825" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="58517" href="NbE.html#28434" class="Function">nf</a> <a id="58520" href="NbE.html#58489" class="Bound">t</a>
<a id="58522" href="NbE.html#58453" class="Function">soundness</a> <a id="58532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58533" href="NbE.html#58533" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="58534" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="58536" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58537" href="NbE.html#58537" class="Bound">T</a><a id="58538" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="58540" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58541" href="NbE.html#58541" class="Bound">t</a><a id="58542" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="58546" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="58551" href="NbE.html#55544" class="Function">fundamental-lemma</a> <a id="58569" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58570" class="Argument">t</a> <a id="58572" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="58574" href="NbE.html#58541" class="Bound">t</a><a id="58575" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="58577" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="58578" href="NbE.html#57553" class="Function">idⓇ↑Γ</a> <a id="58584" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="58585" href="NbE.html#58533" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="58586" class="Symbol">})</a>

  <a id="58605" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="58610" href="NbE.html#43014" class="Function">Ⓡ-==↓</a> <a id="58616" href="NbE.html#58595" class="Bound">tⓇ⟦t⟧↑Γ</a> <a id="58624" href="NbE.html#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">≤-id</a>
